Britain in Singapore, Unremittingly Strengthening Air Defenses, Comprehensive Equipment Eliminates Fears of Enemy Attack, Actively Educating the Public on the Use of Gas Masks 46

Singapore Correspondence The Singapore military authorities now wish to teach 5,000,000 people, speaking a complex variety of dialects and living in narrow alleys and slums, how to practice with gas masks. This is indeed a difficult problem. Although precise arrangements have been made for the protection of the various military strongholds and major enterprises on the island of Singapore, the need to translate the "gas mask teaching method" into Chinese must tax the brains of the Chinese Affairs Commissioners there. Moreover, it is feared that various religious groups among the Asian overseas Chinese may oppose wearing gas masks due to religious superstitions. As for the effects of mustard gas and other types of poisonous gases in the tropics, several experimenters have long tested them, and local manufacturing experts have been engaged to manufacture a mask that can resist the climate here. The government will soon issue a statement discussing the entire air defense problem. It is reported that Singapore will thereafter be placed in the same position as Hong Kong and Columbus, and a large number of cheap gas masks will be stored for distribution. Although Singapore is geographically less likely to be attacked than other major cities in the Far East, the authorities dare not slacken off in all defenses and risk danger. At present, in addition to the original three squadrons of Royal Air Force bombers and comprehensive air defense equipment, Singapore also has a squadron of volunteer air force. Before the end of September this year, this squadron will have six Hawker Audax interceptors listed in the air force and will formulate a procedure to expand the air force in the next three years. (Reuters, 19th)

British-Russian Negotiations Conclude, Financial Agreement Reached, Soviet Loan of 10 Million Pounds, Used to Buy Goods from Britain on Credit 48

(London) It has recently been rumored that negotiations between the Soviet Union and Britain for a loan have been successful. According to financial circles, what has now been established between the two countries is a financial agreement. The government originally planned to announce this at the end of this week, after the adjournment of parliament, to avoid questions from members, but now that rumors have spread widely, it may be forced to issue a formal statement tomorrow. (Havas News Agency, 29th)

(London) Well-informed sources in financial circles here recently announced that negotiations between the Soviet Union and Britain for a loan were concluded last night. The loan amount is 10 million pounds, with a term of ten years and an annual interest rate of 5.5%. (According to reports, these negotiations began six months ago. The proposed method at that time was for Britain to lend 40 million pounds to the Soviet Union for a term of 20 years and an annual interest rate of up to 6%. In addition, the British government would issue domestic bonds of the same amount with an annual interest rate of 2% to cover this loan. The difference in interest rates would be used to settle the debts owed by Imperial Russia to Britain). (Havas News Agency, 29th)

Spanish War Breaks Out, Government Forces Prepare for General Offensive, Rebels Cleared in the Vicinity of Sangcheng in the North, Morale of the People's Front Greatly Boosted 50

(London) News received here today from Andai says that 400 rebels in San Sebastián, who had entrenched themselves in the Lodiola barracks, have surrendered after being bombarded by government troops with machine guns. A column of government troops from San Sebastián and Irun is now besieging Sircos, where the rebel deputy commander General Moore's headquarters are located. Another government force is advancing westward along the coast, occupying and controlling various positions in Vouvidu, which is also one of the important positions occupied by the rebels. The fighting in Madrid has temporarily subsided. It is expected that this calm will not last long. It is reported that the rebel leader General Franco has arrived in Spain from Morocco and intends to lead a large army to attack the capital. Today, according to a public bulletin issued by the government, government forces will take a broad offensive in the coming days in order to quell the rebellion. (Reuters, 28th)

Andai City, France Rumbling artillery fire has recently been heard here, seemingly coming from the direction of San Sebastián (the capital of Guipúzcoa province) in Spain. Yesterday, it was heard that government troops had recovered the villages of Voissen and Lenttria. In light of the news obtained today, this news is probably credible. At present, the rebels in the area from San Sebastián to Irun have been cleared. Peace has also been restored between San Sebastián, Irun, and Voissen. The same is true for Fuenterrabía. The morale of the government troops has been greatly boosted since the surrender of the rebels in Lodiola some time ago. Civilian groups belonging to the People's Front recently paraded through the streets of San Sebastián to celebrate. In addition, the anti-fascist committee organized by Spanish wounded in Toulouse, France, has recently recruited a volunteer team of 50 people, who have crossed the border to return to the country to serve. (Havas News Agency, 29th)

Barcelona Zaragoza is the main base of the rebels in the north. Its location is a major military strong point in Spain, with its perilous terrain, powerful forces (at least ten regiments are stationed there in peacetime), and sophisticated military equipment being second to none in the country. Before the outbreak of the unrest, the rebel leader had already hidden in the area and secretly plotted a change, using this source to incite troops stationed in various parts of the country. Therefore, the government troops are determined to capture the city, and their preparations have been doubled. Thousands of government troops are now waiting in the front line for orders to attack, but it is generally believed that the government authorities will wait until they are sure of victory before ordering an attack, otherwise reckless action would be enough to spoil things. The people of the whole country also know that this fierce battle will determine the outcome of the overall situation and are now looking forward to it. According to some sources, the government troops in Barcelona have dispatched several aircraft and patrol teams today to scout the movements of the enemy, but they have not seen the rebel hideout. Another air force detachment has circled around Huesca. The rebels concentrated there fled in all directions when they heard the sound of the aircraft. In addition, government troops have transferred three artillery teams from Mataró to help in the war. This artillery team is commanded by Captain Medrano, a well-known military leader of the Republican Party, and has recently set off for the front. (Havas News Agency, 24th)

Madrid Government forces and rebels have repeatedly fought fiercely in the northern mountains, advancing and retreating, and have now reached a stage of mutual injury. The rebels have repeatedly failed to attack and are now reorganizing their lines. Government forces still want to take the offensive. Mola, the commander of the rebels in the north, is currently concentrating his troops in Medina-Celia, 95 miles northwest of Madrid, preparing to hold on to the corner. The rebels in the Guadarrama Mountains are holding on to one end of the mountain ridge. Whether the rebels can successfully attack the capital depends on the battle of Guadarrama. The rebels are indeed confident of winning this battle. Government leaders, workers, and leftists often go to the front to encourage the army. (National News Agency, 28th)

Various Frontline War Reports 51

Madrid: In the past twenty-four hours, the situation of the unrest within Spain seems to have slightly calmed, but there are currently still three important battles in progress. The final success or failure will likely be determined in a matter of days or hours. In southwestern Spain, several columns of rebel forces launched from the eastern coast of Spain are advancing towards Seville. The water and electricity supply to Seville has been cut off. In the north, the Barcelona troops have mobilized and are attacking Zaragoza. In the mountains north of Madrid, 12,000 militiamen are continuing fierce battles with General Mola's advance troops. The troops loyal to the government are disregarding the rain and cold weather, making every effort to repel the rebel forces in the Madrid area. The rebel forces there have requested reinforcements. Spanish Army Chief General Costillo, right-wing leader Caballero, and Communist female parliamentarian Ira Lulu visited the government army yesterday. Among the troops, there were many parliamentarians and sixty bullfighting heroes. During the fighting in the mountains near Madrid, a hero named Captain Pique led a suicide squad and destroyed a rebel ammunition depot, causing some of the rebel forces to retreat. The second destination of the government forces, Cordoba, was bombed by several aircraft yesterday. (Reuters, 29th)

Madrid: The official radio station broadcasted the following news last night: (1) A rebel aircraft was shot down by government troops yesterday in the Laroeda area near the port of Malaga in the south. (2) The rebel forces in Seville are in a precarious situation. It is said that the commander of the Andalusia division in Seville, Deliano, is preparing to flee. (3) The Ministry of the Interior announced that workers in the capital should resume work immediately and stated that government aircraft are currently flying to bomb rebel forces in Logrono, south of San Sebastian. (4) The air force commander of Barcelona, ​​Lieutenant Colonel Santino, spent the whole day yesterday training militiamen and distributing firearms in order to go to the front lines to participate in the battle. On the other hand, the Seville rebel radio station denied all the news from the government, especially the news that General Deliano was preparing to flee, and said that a column departing from Seville had captured Huelva without any effort. (in southern Spain). As for Ayamonte (at the mouth of the Guadiana River west of Huelva, on the border between Spain and Portugal), it will also fall soon. Furthermore, the revolutionary army in Galicia in the northwest is extremely dominant. The commander-in-chief of the northern route, General Mola, is gradually advancing towards Pontevedra Province in the northwest according to the planned plan. "It is expected that in a few days, the government army will be unable to resist." (Havas, 28th)

Northern Front War Situation: Government Forces Have Gained an Advantage 52

Saint-Jean-de-Luz, Southern France: According to the war reports from near San Sebastian in northern Spain today, the government forces have gained the upper hand. The rebel forces suffered defeats in the villages of Oyerecun (south of San Sebastian) and Fontarabie (4 kilometers from Irun), and have now retreated towards the Bidassoa River. Earlier, after the rebel forces entrenched in Renteria surrendered to the government forces, the government forces seized a large amount of ammunition stored in the city, and immediately advanced to Oyerecun Village to attack the rebel forces. After a fierce battle, the rebel forces could not hold out and abandoned the village and fled. However, because traffic between the village and Navarre Province (the rebel base) had been cut off, they retreated to Fontarabie. At 6 PM, government troops pursued them, and another fierce battle broke out. The rebel forces were finally defeated and retreated to the Bidassoa River at 7 PM. It is reported that rebel reinforcements are coming from Pamplona (the capital of Navarre), and it is expected that the two sides will still fight soon. However, after these two battles, the position of the government forces in Guipúzcoa Province has been greatly consolidated. (According to previous information, the situation was quite unfavorable for the government forces) (Havas, 28th)

Headquarters of the rebel army on the northern front in Spain: General Mola, commander of the rebel army on the northern front, today launched a charge with a team of elite cavalry against the government army in an attempt to open the Madrid Avenue. Therefore, in the sound of artillery and machine guns, the sound of horses neighing could also be heard. During the close combat, people and animals were not distinguished, and flesh and blood were blurred. The government army's aircraft still flew low and killed many rebel troops. Although General Mola has suffered many setbacks, he is still quite optimistic and said that once he arrives in Madrid, he will reorganize the Spanish army and use a strong military dictatorship to make Spain a great country. "As for the restoration of the monarchy, there is no problem, because this revolution is purely a democratic movement, that is, nationalism opposes internationalism and Spain has always opposed Marxism." Mola also said that he intends to dissolve the left-wing government, and as for what punishment should be given to the leaders who are loyal to the government, it will depend entirely on their respective attitudes. (National Telegram, 28th)

Madrid: Regarding the battle situation in the Guadarrama mountain area north of the capital, it has recently been learned that the rebel forces' ammunition depot has been destroyed by a team of government forces. The government announced that it will issue an order for a general attack soon in order to wipe out the rebel forces and win the final victory. According to what our reporter has learned, the war zone is from Guadarrama Village (40 kilometers north of the capital) and extends along the mountainous area. Currently, transportation from the capital to the village is still convenient. The government army has now decided to begin attacking the Somosierra Pass (70 kilometers from the capital) tomorrow. In addition, on the southern route, the Ministry of the Interior announced that General Miaga led a column of government troops and had arrived near Cordoba (northeast of Seville). The rebel forces in Seville are deserting in large numbers, and many villagers in the suburbs are also carrying weapons to counterattack, so the rebel forces are in a very precarious situation. Traffic between Valencia on the southeastern coast and the capital has been restored. Many trucks loaded with food have recently arrived in the capital from there, so there is no need to worry about the food situation for the people. As for the saying that the rebel forces in Toledo and Aranjuez near the capital have all surrendered, it seems to be premature. Only a small number of those who surrendered are still trapped in the palace there, stubbornly resisting. The government has recently dispatched regular troops and assault teams to encircle and suppress them, in order to force them to surrender quickly and capture them. (Havas, 28th)

Refugees Describe the Tragic Situation on the Battlefield: Rioters Inflict Brutality on Women and Children 55

Saint-Nazaire, France: French refugees who arrived here from Spain today described the brutal acts of the rioters in the battle of San Sebastian a few days ago. A Frenchman who was on vacation in the port said that during the last unrest, a police inspector killed a girl. This time, he was captured by comrades of the Popular Front, killed, and then his body was torn apart and treated like a soccer ball, thrown and played with. A French woman who had lived in the port for many years escaped after her house was looted by the rioters. It is said that the rioters arbitrarily gave live ammunition pistols to children. These children sometimes used pistols to threaten pedestrians as a joke. Sometimes bullets flew out, and innocent people were killed or seriously injured. (Reuters, 28th)

Marseille: Briton Powell led 54 refugees and arrived here today from Barcelona on the British destroyer "Granite." He described a terrible incident. It is said that one day after the government forces and the rebel forces fought fiercely in Barcelona, ​​he went to the street to photograph a destroyed Italian house when six communists suddenly rushed in front of him, with the muzzles of their pistols tightly pressed against his side, and smashed his camera. It was also said that the Red Army leader was waving a large knife, wearing a steel helmet, barefoot, without outerwear, and one of the legs of his shorts had been torn off. The situation was terrible. He was escorted to the Communist Party headquarters. He told them that he was British, but the Red Army insisted that he was German. In order to prove his words, he led them to the hotel and showed them his passport. They began to believe him. Also, an Englishman, Lamb, was implicated in the sudden death of a bookkeeper in a certain tavern and was recently sentenced to 17 years in Barcelona. During the battle in Barcelona this time, the prisons there were opened. Lamb took the opportunity to walk out without being questioned, and then boarded the Granite destroyer, which arrived here today. His parents went to the pier to meet him. (Reuters, 28th)

People from Various Countries Observe the Spanish Situation: The Civil War Will Take Several Weeks Longer: Military Supply is the Main Key to Victory 59

Andaye, Southern France: Observers from various countries, acting as neutrals, observed the Spanish situation last night. All said that neither the government army nor the rebel army had made any substantial progress. Fierce battles did occur in some places, but there were no major changes in the overall situation. However, the militia under the government army has a more complete organization, a more abundant food supply, and the recent establishment of service groups, so the government army seems to be gradually gaining an advantage. But on the one hand, they hope that the rebel army will return and on the other hand, they wait for an appropriate opportunity to defeat them in one fell swoop. Currently, there is still no important development in the war, so this is the reason. According to a reporter from this agency stationed on the border between France and Spain, the rebel army was defeated in the battle of Oyerecun a few days ago, and the battle was very fierce. The two sides even fought hand-to-hand. The sound of artillery at night was still deafening. According to the latest news, after this defeat of the rebel army, the situation in Guipuzcoa Province seems to be advantageous for the government army. As for the radio broadcasts issued by the wireless stations of both sides, they are still optimistic. However, according to the speculation of observers from various countries, the end of the Spanish Civil War still has a long way to go. (Havas, 29th)

Whether the government army or the rebel army will win depends on the military supply. The tough right-wing newspaper reported that the French government refused to sell aircraft to the Spanish Republican government last week. The embassy is now trying to find other ways to achieve its goal. It is said that there are several old-fashioned 1929 aircraft stored in the Etampes airfield, which originally belonged to the French Air Force, but because the style has become obsolete, the manufacturers will bid to recover them and sell them to Spain as civilian aircraft. Future Five-Nation Conference: Italy is Preparing to Participate: Germany Has No Concrete Expression 62

Now that these conditions have been met, there is no possibility of shirking responsibility. As for Germany, when the ambassadors of the United Kingdom, France, and Belgium delivered the invitation to participate in the Five-Nation Conference to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the country, the Director of Political Affairs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Digov, expressed goodwill, but the country has not yet put forward a concrete answer as to whether or not to participate. Although this statement has not been confirmed by officials, political figures generally believe it is credible. Italy will have no objection to this claim of Germany and will follow suit. Government officials now hope that Germany will participate in the Five-Nation Conference to the utmost extent, so they believe that Chamberlain's anti-German remarks in the House of Commons yesterday were inappropriate. Because up to now, the main weapon of German foreign policy has been to be self-sufficient and not to cooperate with other countries. Chamberlain's remarks yesterday may give the country an excuse to continue to adopt an isolation policy, which is the most feared by the United Kingdom. Political figures and newspapers are refraining from criticizing Chamberlain's speech, and the general purpose is to reduce its importance and prevent Germany from paying attention to it. Relations Between Germany and Czechoslovakia: Negotiate a Ten-Year Non-Aggression Treaty: Three Conditions as Exchange 63

(London) Regarding the relations between Germany and Czechoslovakia, the diplomatic reporter of the Morning Post recently stated, "As far as I know, Germany will take action in a short period of time. What is the action? It is to propose to Czechoslovakia the conclusion of a ten-year non-aggression treaty, with the following three items as exchange conditions. This condition, one is that the wishes of the German minorities in Czechoslovakia must be satisfied. Two is the establishment of a federal system, and the granting of autonomous rights to German minorities. Three is that the mutual assistance treaty concluded between Czechoslovakia and the Soviet Union must be abandoned. This proposition has been informally put forward by the leader of the German minority in Czechoslovakia, that is, the leader of the Sudeten German Party of the Germanism School, Hanlun (who recently visited the United Kingdom). If this can be realized, then the Czech problem can be solved after the Austrian problem. In addition, the ten-year non-aggression treaty concluded between Poland and Germany is also continuously valid. In this way, German Führer Hitler has sufficient reason to demand that the scope of the future Five-Nation Conference be restricted and not expanded. However, the Czechoslovak authorities may not necessarily accept Hitler's claim regarding the country's minorities, because as far as I (the newspaper's diplomatic reporter claims) know, the Czechoslovak government is willing to consider the legitimate wishes of the German minority, but it believes that the federal system is difficult to implement. " (Havas, 29th)

New Invention by Japanese Professor: Underwater Wireless Telephone; To Be Used for Communication Between Submarines 68

(Tokyo) Dr. Yamahira Ichizo, a professor at Tohoku Imperial University in Japan, recently invented an underwater wireless telephone. As a result of a public demonstration conducted off the port of Shiogama the other day, the clarity of the voice was no less than that of wired or wireless telephones. It was found that the current used on that day was only 5 watts, yet it was able to communicate freely in water at a distance of 500 meters. Therefore, if a high degree of power is used, it will undoubtedly be successful for long-distance communication. The Japanese Navy is paying close attention to this and plans to apply it immediately to communication between submarines. (28th, China United Press)

After Jiang Zhicheng, director of the Lushan Administration Bureau, and British Consul Morse signed an agreement on New Year's Day this year to recover all the leased land on the mountain, there was a proposal to build a national park. Recently, central leaders and military and political figures have gathered in Lushan, making Lushan once again a political center, adding a lot of color to the famous mountain. Currently, various Yuan, Ministries, and Commissions have established offices in Lushan for summer work. The investigation is as follows:

The office is located at No. 17 Yishengwa. Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi's villa is at No. 51, and the office is located at No. 50. Hankou Workers' Leader Wang Jinxia Shot; Seriously Injured; One Assailant Captured on the Spot; Central People's Training Committee Telegraphed Hankou to Inquire About the Incident 83

Hankou Correspondence: Wang Jinxia, director of the Hankou Dockworkers' Union, once represented Hankou at the National Assembly and also represented China at the 19th International Labor Conference last year. After returning from Europe, he resumed his original position. As a dockworker, he has been the leader of the Hankou labor community for nine years. Recently, he was suddenly shot and seriously injured, and his life may be in danger. It is said that there are more than twenty assailants, and only one was captured on the spot. It is believed to be an organized and planned action. After the incident occurred, society paid close attention to it. The Central People's Training Department of the Kuomintang telegraphed the Hankou Municipal Party Department to inquire about the incident for verification. The reporter visited Wang and saw that his face was red and swollen, his upper lip was broken by an iron rod, his hands and feet were bandaged, and he was spitting blood from his mouth. Due to the severity of his injuries, he could not talk much. He showed me the report submitted to the Central Standing Committee and the Central People's Training Department, which stated: "Hu Dingshan, the executive director of the union, Shi Zhonglin, a dismissed employee of the dock management office, Yuan Zhihua, a clerk of the 13th branch of the dock, and the gangsters Liu Musheng, Yi Xiangtai, and Li Haigou, etc., secretly formed a secret organization called the Patriotic Salvation Corps, intending to sabotage the labor movement. Because I refused to be used by them, they repeatedly threatened me and sent letters of intimidation through Shi Zhonglin twice, which I ignored. On the morning of June 16th, Shi Zhonglin asked me to talk. At 9:00 am that morning, Shi Zhonglin, Hu Dingshan, and Huang Huashan, director of the dockworkers' union, came to my house. Shi raised several points: 1. The National Assembly is approaching, and some people in our organization are running for election. Please do not hinder our progress. If you continue to oppress the lower-level comrades, we will be sorry for you. 2. Fang Duanru, a clerk in the 3rd branch, should be dismissed immediately and replaced by Xiao Zhenxian. 3. Please join the Patriotic Salvation Corps organized by us." The wording was strict, and he waited for a reply. I replied that everyone has the freedom to run for election to the National Assembly and cannot be hindered by others. I have never oppressed anyone. Fang Duanru, a clerk in the 3rd branch, was approved by the 12th meeting of the council on June 10th, and I have no power to dismiss him. As for joining the Patriotic Salvation Corps, because I am a member of the Kuomintang, I cannot join any political organization other than the Kuomintang. Seeing that their threats were unsuccessful and knowing that they could not be subdued by coercion or inducement, they conspired to kill me. At 12:30 pm on the 18th of this month, they gathered more than twenty people, all armed with iron weapons, and ambushed on both sides of Fu Dong Er Road and in the teahouse. When I was passing by on my way home from the union, Shi, Hu, and others rushed forward and dragged me to the ground. The weapons came down together, and I was covered in injuries, trying to kill me. Fortunately, neighbors and the staff of the dockworkers' union and the police heard the sound and gathered, and they fled. The police captured the murderer Liu Musheng on the spot and transferred him to the court. I was admitted to Xiehe Hospital for treatment and have been vomiting blood ever since. I cannot eat or drink, and I am delirious. My injuries are getting worse and worse, and my life is in danger. There are hospital injury reports to prove it. Hu and others are either current executive directors or former employees. They are so lawless. I urge you to quickly order the Wuhan Party, government, military, and police agencies to arrest Hu and others and severely punish them according to law, and thoroughly investigate their illegal organization to eliminate hidden dangers, maintain the labor movement, and protect the safety of party members' lives." (July 28)

Miscellaneous Writings from Rural Hubei 84

— Special Correspondent for this Newspaper, Cheng Jun

(Twenty-Two) Two Days in Yingcheng (Part One)

Yingcheng is located in central Hubei, 117 kilometers from Wuhan. It is famous both domestically and internationally for its gypsum and salt production, along with hot springs and lingzhi mushrooms, collectively known as the "Three Treasures." Due to the urgency of my business, I was unable to fulfill my desire for sightseeing. On July 25th, the Provincial Highway Bureau hosted a press tour to inspect the construction of the Hanyi Road, giving me the opportunity to visit. I traveled around the gypsum mines and salt fields, rural villages and towns, admiring the immortal herbs, truly blessed with spiritual energy, and sampling the warm waters, comparable to those of Huaqing Palace. People marveled at its wonders, and I felt my body further nourished. I record my journey to share with readers.

Things Seen and Heard Along the Way

On July 25th, at 4 p.m., I and a dozen colleagues gathered at Jianghan Customs and boarded a vehicle to set off along Hanyi Road. Zhu Yuanqing, Secretary of the Provincial Highway Bureau, Yi Rong, the section chief of the Western Hubei section, and others accompanied us. Passing through Qiaokou, Duoluokou, and X溝, we were still within the jurisdiction of Wuhan. Recalling the floods of last year, the areas of Duoluokou and X溝 were submerged in vast waters, and the roads were completely destroyed. It hasn't been long since then, but they have already been repaired. The road surface and bridges have been completely renewed. Further west, we reached Xin'andu, belonging to Hanchuan County. Ferries were used to transport the vehicles across the river, as if traveling on flat ground. Manjiagang is the intersection of Hanchuan, Yunmeng, and Xiaogan counties, commonly known as the "Three No-Man's Land." Changfapu is a relatively large town, with the east side of the river belonging to Yunmeng and the west side belonging to Yingcheng. Similar to Manjiagang, it required crossing by boat. Further west, we arrived in Yingcheng County. Due to the pre-arranged itinerary, we did not disembark and crossed the county river, making this our fourth river crossing. Soon after, we reached Zaoshi, with thousands of houses, tall buildings, and mansions coming into view. This place belongs to Tianmen. In previous years, it was the area where He Long, Duan Dechang, and other bandits roamed. Because the bandits regarded it as a nest, it was not burned down. Now, a city gate called Taiping Gate (Peace Gate) has been built to commemorate the chaos. At the Sanwen intersection beside the train station, there were five members of the local militia team standing guard with spears. One of them had a pensive face and was over sixty years old. The others were thirteen or fourteen years old, with one underaged member only about ten years old. The banner read "Tianmen Sixth District, Seventy-Third Bao (Neighborhood) Squad." Apart from one who could be considered a strong man, the other four were either old or weak. Using them to defend against bandits is truly a mockery of the world. Further ahead, the road diverged. Turning north, we quickly reached Wenquan (Hot Spring) Township, which is a famous scenic spot of Yingcheng. It was already dusk, and the sound of frogs filled the fields. Mountain children played with calves, and the towering trees seemed to touch the sky, making one feel as if they were in a painting. From Hankou to Zaoshi, we passed through six counties, which is the eastern section of Hanyi Road. The road was built on the roadbed of the Chuanhan Railway. Each station along the way has a platform, and the bridge piers and culverts all have foundations. With the Highway Bureau's maintenance, the road surface is paved with stone, as smooth as a whetstone. Driving is safe and unhindered by wind or rain. Among all the highways in the province, it is undoubtedly the best. Besides the road improvement, which was quite satisfactory, the agricultural products seen along the way, such as cotton, rice, and sorghum, were all thriving. It was said that the rice in Yingcheng even had double ears (two grains per stalk), promising a good harvest. I couldn't help but feel excited.

Trying the Baths at Tangchi (Hot Spring Pool)

Tangchi is located west of Yingcheng County, surrounded by mountains and forests, with a tranquil and secluded landscape. There are three hot springs, each several feet apart. The area has a small village named after the hot springs. The water from the hot springs comes from deep underground and gushes upwards, with a slight sulfurous odor, boiling year-round, and a very abundant source. They were formerly divided into the First Pool, Second Pool, and Third Pool. Villagers all draw water into their homes for bathing, which can cure skin diseases. It has been famous since the Sui Dynasty. The Geography section of the Book of Sui mentions, "Yingyang has hot springs," referring to this place. Throughout history, famous figures have written poems about this place. The most famous is Li Bai. Li Bai's poem says, "The goddess disappeared into the secluded realm, the hot spring baths the great river. Yin and Yang unite the burning charcoal, and creation opens the spiritual spring. The bottom of the pool glows with crimson fire, and the sand emits pure smoke. Boiling pearls shine like the bright moon, and the bright mirror reflects the empty sky. The fragrance of orchids fills the air, and the color of peach blossoms is vibrant. A close inspection reveals myriad differences, and a secret passage connects seven marshes. Healing wounds is unsurpassed, and transformation fulfills the Tao. The rinsing water is clear and refreshing, and drying hair is done near the babbling stream. It is scattered down the Chu kingdom and divided to irrigate Song Yu's fields. It could be used to serve imperial visits, but alas, it is isolated and remote. Only following the water heading towards the court, it offers its meager contribution to the sea." Also, Qing Dynasty poet Xi Dazhuang wrote, "Ten thousand bushels of flowing spring everywhere bring spring, and from the beginning, its heat does not depend on people. The source is lively and the waves are misty, and heaven bestows on us a good place to cleanse ourselves. Lush water mist fills the air, and a harmonious vitality wants to penetrate the skin. Everywhere, the grace of the waves is warm, as if one is in the Phoenix Pool. Washing away worldly dust is also pleasing, and drying hair in the breeze as the sun sets. Surprisingly reciting the verses of Qinglian (Li Bai), I look up at the white clouds with deep admiration for the past." Currently, Tangchi has renovated bathrooms and a beautiful hotel for tourists to bathe and stay. I unpacked in the hotel and took a bath at night, enjoying the clear waves immensely. After the bath, I immediately felt a breeze under my armpits, with a lightness as if wanting to ascend to immortality. On the morning of the 26th, I went for another bath and visited the First Pool and Second Pool. Hot air steamed, condensing into fog. Looking down, the boiling springs surged upwards, like drops of pearls. On one side of the First Pool, the water was cool and clear, with fish and shrimp swimming in it, truly showing the wonders of creation.

Rural Survey

Tangchi itself is a rural village, and a rural improvement experimental zone has been established, dividing into agricultural-forestry cooperation, militia training, popular night schools, elementary school, medicine, and animal husbandry departments, with the main goals of implementing rural education, cultivating farmers' morals, improving farming skills, and increasing agricultural and forestry production. Since its establishment in the 23rd year (of the Republic), in the first year, over eighty mu of land was rented for cultivation, and the harvest was doubled compared to before. After the 24th year, the focus was on public training for self-defense, emphasizing water conservancy, expanding afforestation, textile, rice milling, oil pressing, and animal husbandry industries, as well as handling credit and marketing cooperation, in order to adjust the rural economy. The results have been quite impressive. Former Provincial Committee member and Director of the Construction Department, Li Fan, lives here after leaving office, also working on rural reconstruction. In Tangchi, there are windmills and granaries, etc. The windmills are used to remove chaff, and the granaries are used for storage, all to benefit the farmers, and no fees are charged. Li also bought 500 mu of land at Guanyin Rock, 30 li from here, and developed it into a farm. Every day, he wears a straw hat and goes barefoot, traveling 60 li back and forth, personally inspecting the fields once, not considering it a hardship. He is also an extraordinary person. As for the general situation of the rural areas in the whole county, after investigation and interviews, the whole area has more fields than land, with rice, wheat, and beans as the main agricultural products, followed by sesame, and then cotton. The area is measured in dan and dou (traditional units of volume), and transactions are based on qiu (mounds) and duan (sections). Roughly two dou and five, are implicitly equal to one mu (a unit of area). Upper-grade fields produce two shi (another unit of volume) of wheat and three shi of grain per mu. Middle-grade fields produce one shi and six dou of wheat and two shi and five dou of grain. Lower-grade fields produce one shi and two dou of wheat and two shi of grain. During the off-season, farmers all have side jobs. Farmers in the northwest mostly transport gypsum and salt with mules and horses, or work as laborers in the salt mines. Farmers in the east mostly go to Wuhan to sell their labor. Those in the south mostly fish and gather firewood. Fields are divided into six grades, and regular and supplementary taxes are paid together. The highest is 4 jiao and 7 fen per mu, and the lowest is 3 jiao and 0.8 li.

A Glimpse of the County Seat

At noon on the 26th, we left Tangchi and returned, traveling 30 li to Yingcheng County. We got off the car and entered the city. The streets were relatively clean. There were the Yingcheng Yinhao Bank, Weizhang Hospital, Shengjia Jewelry Store, Xinguang Photo Studio, Yingyi Restaurant, etc. Educational institutions included a junior high school, and judicial institutions included a local court. The amusement venue was Zhongshan Park. Inside the park was a memorial pavilion commemorating the patriotic student movement last year, which resulted in an incident due to misunderstandings. I heard that lingzhi mushrooms were currently stored in the library of the People's Education Center, so I made a special trip to visit. The center was located on the old site of the Confucian temple, with ancient cypress trees reaching the sky and green shade covering the ground. With the introduction of Zhang Yuezhong, the section chief of the county government, I met the director of the center, Peng Wenbin, and was able to see the lingzhi mushrooms. They were produced in Wujia Mountain. They had no peculiar smell. The mushroom had a single stem and was shaped like a ruyi (a curved decorative object symbolizing good fortune), with a crimson color. It is commonly said that consuming it can lead to immortality. Although this is not credible, it is still a special species. The center also displayed iron cannons from the seventh and eighth years of the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, weighing 501 jin each, which had historical significance. There was also a tombstone of General Huang from the second year of Emperor Taikang of the Xia Dynasty, which was unearthed at Guifeng Temple last spring. Then, I went to the county government to visit County Magistrate Liu Lixin. He led us to visit the entire office. The most notable were the male and female prisons. The prisons were clean, with ample lighting, and equipped with bathhouses and toilets. There were 50 male prisoners and only 3 female prisoners. Most of the crimes were related to marital disputes. The male prisoners were divided into groups to work, sewing clothes and husking rice, each doing their job. Seeing reporters entering the prison for a visit, they all stood up automatically, showing good manners, indicating that they had received education. According to County Magistrate Liu, the major products of the county are gypsum, salt, local cloth, and grain. The annual gypsum production is over 400,000 tai (loads), worth 1.5 to 1.6 million yuan. The salt production is 140,000 to 150,000 dan, worth 1.6 million yuan. The local cloth production is 3,000 rolls, with 32 pi (bolts) per roll, each pi worth 1 yuan, totaling 10,000 yuan. The living conditions of the rural people are relatively frugal, but the merchants in the city are concentrated here due to the gypsum and salt industries, and their lives are beyond the norm. The children of wealthy families also live very extravagantly. The local customs have become accustomed to extravagance. Efforts are currently being made to correct this. Education in the whole county is relatively developed. There is Xihe Junior High School, an affiliated county-run simplified normal school class, five complete elementary schools, 54 primary schools, one vocational school for women, 15 mobile folk schools, one library, five people's education centers, and five circulating library depots. Gypsum and salt merchants bear a heavy burden of local surtaxes, such as education funds, security funds, and county government funds, which rely on this donation for subsidies, and the education funds rely on it for funding. (Sent from Hankou on the 26th)

Troops Stationed in Chaozhou and Meizhou Awaiting Orders for Post-Conflict Arrangements; Huang Yanzhen and Huang Renhuan Arrived in the Provincial Capital to Seek Instructions; Martial Law Has Also Been Lifted in Chao'an and Shantou 85

Shantou Correspondence: In the beginning of Chen Jitang's resignation, the troops stationed in the Dongjiang and Hanjiang regions were frequently mobilized, and rumors were rampant. Eventually, after Yu Hanmou arrived in Guangzhou and the situation stabilized, the various armies received orders from superiors to remain stationed in their original defenses and not move without authorization. The 7th and 8th Divisions of the 3rd Army were therefore stationed in the upper reaches of the Dongjiang River, while Army Commander Huang Yanzhen returned to the provincial capital to meet with Yu, seeking instructions on the issue of downsizing and stationing troops. Army Commander Huang Renhuan of the 4th Army and East District Committee Member Li Yukun also went to the provincial capital on the 23rd, awaiting orders to attend meetings to discuss military post-conflict arrangements. Furthermore, Huang Renhuan's troops shortened their defensive line starting this month, moving the army headquarters from Meixian County to Laolong in the upper reaches of the Dongjiang River. The 10th Division, led by Zeng Youren, retreated from Jiaoling and Meixian to the mountains of Wuhua, stationed in Anliu and Hepo, and was mutually vigilant with the 9th Division stationed in Dianning. The 11th Division, led by Yan Tingyu, was stationed in Fengshun City. The 12th Division, led by Chen Hanguang, was transferred to the Xijiang South Road, leaving only the regiment led by Deputy Division Commander Peng Zhifang stationed in Chao'an City. When the 3rd and 4th Armies were redeployed, rumors were rampant in various places, and counties, districts, and villages imposed martial law. Subsequently, on the 22nd, Huang Renhuan telegraphed the division commanders from the provincial capital, ordering them to remain in place and await orders, which somewhat eased the situation. On the 23rd, martial law was also lifted in Shantou, but military police still jointly patrolled the city in armed vehicles, or searched travelers at wharves and train stations. Hotels, gambling houses, and opium dens were still subject to inspections. The same was true in Chao'an. However, people's hearts were greatly calmed. (24th)

Japanese in the Northeast Promote a New Agricultural Policy; Establish a Fundamental Plan for Agricultural Development; In Reality, Preparing for War Against Soviet Russia 86

Changchun Correspondence: Since the Japanese created a puppet regime in the Northeast, all kinds of construction work have been completely controlled by the Japanese. According to their claims, the first phase of work has come to an end. From now on, they will actively start the second phase of economic construction work, which can exert a great effect on the Soviet Union in terms of national defense. Therefore, the Japanese ordered the authorities of various departments of the puppet regime to implement mobilization preparations. Their concrete construction policy, especially the fundamental plan for developing agriculture, has been thoroughly researched in advance. Now, the puppet Ministry of Industry, Ministry of Civil Affairs, Ministry of Mongolian Affairs, and related departments are ordered to proceed according to this policy. The main plan is roughly as follows:

Main Plan

(1) To make the national agricultural experiment institutions complete and enriched. (2) To implement the universal deployment of agricultural instructors stationed in each county. (3) To make the agricultural survey institutions complete and enriched. (4) To cultivate specialized agricultural guidance talents. (5) To organize the national agricultural groups. (6) To perfect the agricultural observation network. (7) To enrich the local industrial encouragement facilities. (8) To construct model villages. (9) To establish an agricultural financial system. (10) To expand the sales channels for special products. (11) To set up agricultural warehouses. (12) To encourage the farmers' autonomous economy. Among the above plans, the increase of the main agricultural crops such as soybeans, sorghum, millet, corn, wheat, cotton, tobacco, and sugar beets is the first step of the work elements.

Agricultural Group Organization

For the convenience of control, the Japanese are implementing their common association doctrine, as the foundation for farmers to become self-reliant. Based on the general idea of ​​this beautiful name, they will order the agricultural groups in various places in the Northeast to implement forceful reorganization, that is, to organize farmers' groups with the farmers' associations as units, and to establish simple common organizations according to the establishment of the district and village system. The farmers' associations will then take a middle position to correct the repayment method, and strive to prevent the exhaustion of finance, and generally privately engage in young seedlings trading and high-interest loans. Currently, the Japanese believe that this plan is the most brilliant.

Warehouse Establishment

In the future, the widespread establishment of agricultural warehouses in various places is, in reality, preparing for food for the war against the Soviet Union, while the Japanese superficially claim to stabilize finance, prevent the general sale of agricultural products and young seedlings trading, and generally engage in sales and other matters, giving the general farmers the benefits they deserve. And first in North Manchuria, in the branches of the puppet Central Bank, the recognized grain stacks and the necessary places for grain inspection, a total of ten places, the above-mentioned agricultural warehouses will be set up to consolidate the agricultural foundation, and then spread to various parts of the Northeast. Regarding the above items, they are now proceeding step by step, and the puppet Ministry of Industry is actively preparing for the formulation of the Farmers' Association Law and the Agricultural Warehouse Law, and it is expected to be announced and implemented at the latest within this year. If so, after the implementation of the above-mentioned new agricultural policy, the shortcomings of the past unregulated agricultural product prices and insufficient supply in the Northeast can be swept away, and the rural situation and the agricultural foundation will become more consolidated.

Songjiang: The Jinshan Mouth Robbery Case Solved 87

The home of farmer Pan Jinhuo, in the 6th Jia of the 2nd Bao of the 8th District of Punan (Jinshan Mouth) in the county, was robbed on the evening of the 22nd by seven bandits speaking a local dialect. One person was posted outside as a lookout, while the rest broke through the stove door and entered the house. They tied up Jinhuo's mother with a rope and forced her to reveal where the silver was hidden. Then they overturned boxes and cabinets, searching thoroughly. They escaped with their loot after half an hour, including cotton, broad beans, clothing, and other items. The victim was afraid of incurring the bandits' resentment and did not dare to report to the authorities. It was not until the 26th that the chief of the Shanyang Patrol Station heard about the incident and went to investigate with the security team. According to people in the village, one of the six bandits seemed to be Pan Abu from the village, which raised suspicions of him being an accomplice. Qin Shihuan, the squad leader of the 1st Platoon of the 12th Brigade of the garrison security force stationed in the mountains, immediately led soldiers to arrest Pan Abu in Dongmen Township. The patrol station also reported the results of the investigation, along with a list of lost items, to the bureau to request assistance in apprehending the remaining bandits.

Wuxi: Rice Prices Gradually Decline 88

Since the beginning of summer this year, the climate has been suitable, with timely rainfall, which has greatly benefited the farmland. The local grain market has abundant inventory, and sales are slow. In addition, new xian rice from Zhejiang and Anhui will soon be on the market. Therefore, grain merchants' sentiments have greatly softened, and market prices have gradually declined. Qingbai japonica rice has fallen to 9.1 yuan, a decrease of more than 1 yuan compared to rice prices a few months ago. Currently, the rice crops in the four rural areas are generally thriving. The harvest in the future will surely be bountiful. Therefore, overall, the market is expected to continue to decline. As for the price of wheat, the flour mills have suffered losses due to this year's wet wheat kernels. As a result, operations have been intermittent, and market prices have also become depressed. Yesterday, the price of each bag fell by 2 jiao. In addition, the price of flour has fallen by 6 fen per bag in three or four days. Yesterday's prices were 3.09 yuan per bag for Green Mountain Deer flour and 2.99 yuan per bag for Red Mountain Deer flour.

The Chunyun Smuggling Case Unfolds Again 89

After the railway bureau discovered that the station master, luggage room director, and other staff members of the local railway station had organized a smuggling ring, it dismissed and disciplined the station masters and other related personnel on the 2nd of this month. However, station masters Shi, Wang, and Zhou, as well as freight yard director Ma Ziqing, and yard supervisor Luo Xingchu, among others, petitioned the bureau to appeal their cases. After the management bureau repeatedly sent people to Wuxi to investigate, the truth of the case began to emerge. It is now known that the police department of the two railway lines, because the former section chief of the second section stationed in Wuxi, Zou Yuou, was also related to the main suspect in the smuggling case, Wang Xingen, not only dismissed him, but also discovered that patrolman Liu Ayun of the section was also suspected of participating in smuggling. Therefore, it specifically telegraphed section chief Chen Jie yesterday, ordering him to place Liu Ayun under supervision, and sent two police officers to escort him to Shanghai for interrogation. It is heard that Wang Xingen, the main culprit in the case, has completed his sentence after being dealt with by the police department and has now regained his freedom.

Yangzhou: Altered Stamp Imprint Leads to Tax Collection 90

When Jiangdu County Government processed land declarations and corrections, it was discovered that Chen Ronghe, who held a land ownership certificate for 12.5 mu, had altered the receipt after paying taxes. In the spring, Chen entrusted Ren Mao to file the declaration on his behalf. Ren only filled in 2.2 mu and earned a fine of 1 yuan (calculated at 1 jiao per mu), and only paid 3 jiao. Afterwards, he added the characters "二十" (twenty) to the number of mu, and the characters "一元" (one yuan) to the fine of 3 jiao. Yesterday (the 27th), when Chen came to check the receipt, the discrepancy was discovered. Section Chief Shen found out and summoned Ren for interrogation. Ren confessed without hesitation. He was ordered to be shackled and displayed in front of the main hall granary as a warning, and then sent to the court for legal proceedings.

Where is the Hirota Cabinet Going? (9) 91

— Jia He

Currently, the military and Hirota are heading towards a hand-to-hand struggle, no matter which way you look at it. Reality demands a reckoning of balanced forces. If Hirota continues to take an ambiguous attitude, he will inevitably be rejected by the military. If he follows the military, the zaibatsu (financial conglomerates) will whip him from behind. An open opposition to the military would allow the military to appeal to the Japanese people if their demands are not met. They can point out that Hirota's cabinet's "renovation of all administration" is not true to its name. They can movingly accuse Hirota of forgetting the suffering of the people, failing to accept the military's proposals, and failing to reduce the various burdens of the people. They can also attack Hirota for not establishing a Ministry of Health and neglecting the alarming figures of conscription physical examinations – during the years of Taisho 11 to 15 (1922-1926), the number of conscripts who failed the examination was 250 per thousand, which increased to 350 per thousand during the years of Showa 2 to 7 (1927-1932), and increased again to 400 per thousand the year before last. Finally, they can create another world-shocking event.

There are already many facts that hint to us that the military may rise again. The most important one is that the class division in the country is becoming more obvious. In the past, cabinet member Maeda publicly called on the established political parties to unite and confront the Social Mass Party. Now, due to the strengthening of the left wing, perhaps yesterday's hope can prompt the Japanese ruling class to implement it. Because the All-Japan Federation of Trade Unions, Tokyo Exchange and other eight groups have established the Labor and Peasant Proletarian Council, backed by the Tokyo Exchange anti-Social Mass Party faction, and elected Kato Kanju as the permanent chairman and Suzuki Mosaburo as the secretary-general, as a prelude to the grand union of the legal left wing. Although the strength is weak, it is no longer a heap of loose sand as before. Moreover, the workers in Osaka, under the slogan of "United Front," also have the possibility of breaking the traditional prejudices and uniting. On July 4, Kato dissolved the Labor and Peasant Proletarian Council and began to establish a new, left-leaning, anti-fascist proletarian party, then the power will be even stronger.

On the other hand, the right wing, centered on Yoshida Masuzo of the Japan Production Party, has long called for a patriotic political alliance, Hyogo Prefecture Patriotic Society, New Japan National League, etc., to hold a joint promotion symposium for all patriotic political parties in Osaka. On June 20, another conference was held, with more than 200 representatives wanting to form a "Restoration Party." This is exactly the opposite of Kato's actions. This shows that Hirota's policy is not only unable to embark on the middle way, but also increasingly promotes the division between the left and right wings. The clearer the division, the weaker the foundation for the existence of middle-type, transitional cabinets, and the shorter the life of the Hirota cabinet. When the left wing evolves from verbal propaganda to action, the military will be an indispensable tool for the Japanese ruling class. At that time, the Hirota cabinet will either give way to more radical people, or it will have to undergo another self-denial.

Perhaps it is already in such a gradual process, but when will the mutation occur? That depends on the ebb and flow of the forces of the various classes within Japan, the international situation, and the strength of the Chinese nation's resistance. (The End)

Pinghu: All Shops Closed in Xin Cang Town 92

Xin Cang Town in this county suddenly declared a market strike on the 22nd of this month. According to the investigation by the Party Department, the Xin Cang District Office was abusing its power and acting arbitrarily. If someone led an ox past its door, and the ox accidentally defecated, the person leading the ox would be arrested, beaten, and fined heavily, and the ox would also be severely beaten. The office set up a smoking cessation center. The staff in the center provided meals to the offenders, but did not pay a single penny for more than two months. When the chef refused to continue contracting, he was arrested and detained in the office. The guarantor of the chef was questioned by the chef's side, and he went to the director of the office to intercede, but he was also arrested and detained. After several days, he was released after the elder Zhou Guiting went to plead for him. The debt was still not paid. This caused resentment everywhere. After the city strictly prohibited shirtless men, Xin Cang immediately followed suit. Those who were arrested for being shirtless were whipped with rattan canes, detained in the office overnight, and fined one yuan before being released. They were not given undershirts like in the city area. A police officer patrolling the street, or so it was said to be the director of the office himself, saw a shirtless man across the river and dug up a stone locust tree on the road and threw it with all his might. On the 22nd, a police officer with a loaded gun box was looking for shirtless people. He broke into He Kang Sauce Garden and ordered all the workers, who were all shirtless, to stop working, which led to a dispute. Someone shouted in the street to quickly close the market, which was immediately echoed by everyone, and the market was closed on the spot. The county government's efforts to persuade were ineffective. On the 24th, the county Party Department sent people to investigate. Tens of thousands of people welcomed them at the pre-station. When they arrived at the town, the victims bared their arms to show their wounds. The staff of the Party Department then decided that the prohibition of shirtless men should wait until the Pinghu New Transport Branch decides on a unified method before it is promoted uniformly throughout the county. The director of the office agreed, and Xin Cang opened all shops in the town on the 25th.

Jiaxing: Hangzhou Customs Investigates Smuggling 93

The Jiaxing Jiahe Cloth Factory was found by the county investigation team to have 22 boxes of Japanese bleaching powder. Because there were no separate transport documents, it was considered smuggled goods. After sealing them up, it reported to the county government for handling. Subsequently, Zhou Yuqing, the manager of the factory, went to Shanghai to obtain the permit and handed it over to the county. The county sent a letter to the Jianghai Customs, requesting it to investigate and handle the case based on the handling process of the county. It is now known that after the Provincial Party Department received the report from the County Party Department on this case, it sent Fa Guangyu from the Hangzhou Customs on the 28th to Jiaxing by car. He first went to the County Chamber of Commerce to investigate everything. Then, the chamber sent Secretary Shi to accompany him to the Party and government agencies to solicit opinions. Finally, he went to the Jiahe Cloth Factory to conduct an on-site investigation. Fa Guangyu returned to Hangzhou on the same day to report.

Hangzhou: Taking Over Local Bank 94

The Ministry of Finance has ordered the Bank of China to take over the issuance part of the Zhejiang Local Bank. Recently, Xu Enpei, the general manager of the Local Bank, went to Shanghai, and the procedures and methods for the takeover have been negotiated with the Bank of China authorities. After Xu returns to Hangzhou, the takeover will begin at the beginning of next month.

Xiaoshan: Son Dies, Parents Commit Suicide 95

Zheng Bingyan, a resident of Zunyi Bridge, located at the border of Xiao and Shao [counties], was in his twilight years. He had only one son, A Yuan, who worked as a machinist in Hangzhou. Each year, he would send money home to support the family, which they were quite content with. Unexpectedly, on the 27th of this month, his son suddenly contracted an epidemic and died in Hangzhou. The machine shop immediately informed Zheng Bingyan and instructed him to come to Hangzhou to collect the body. Upon hearing the news, Bingyan was in a state of bewilderment. In the afternoon, he threw himself into the river and committed suicide. He was rescued by people, but he had already died. His wife, Madam Yu, was of similar age. Upon hearing that her son had died and her husband had also committed suicide, she took advantage of a moment when no one was watching in the evening and hanged herself. Fortunately, neighbors and relatives witnessed this tragedy and helped arrange the funeral.

Shanghai Cultural Organizations Sternly Advise Li Bai 96

The Guomin She [National Society] reports that the China Cultural Construction Association and 55 other cultural organizations, considering that the Central Government has been lenient and tolerant regarding the recent unrest in Guangdong and Guangxi, not pursuing the matter rigorously and even granting Li Bai a new position, yet up to now, Li Bai has not only failed to express frankness but is also rumored to be resisting orders. Yesterday, they sent a telegram of stern advice and also sent a telegram to Chairman Lin and Chairman Chiang, urging them to issue strict orders for service. The original telegram is excerpted below:

Telegram to Li Bai

"Most Urgent. Honored Sirs Li Delin [Zongren] and Bai Jiansheng [Chongxi] of Nanning: It is noted that you have resorted to arms and caused disturbances with the aid of foreign powers. If judged according to party discipline and national law, how could you defend yourselves and apologize to the people of the nation? However, the Central Government, recognizing your past contributions to the revolution, albeit with some merit, cherishes benevolence and urges you to improve yourselves. Therefore, you have been granted the positions of Standing Committee Member of the Military Affairs Commission and Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government to encourage and observe future actions. However, since the announcement of the new appointments, many days have passed, and your attitude remains ambiguous. Reports even suggest that you are inviting wolves into the house and resisting orders. Such obstinate behavior is deeply alarming. Therefore, a special telegram is sent to offer sincere advice. It is hoped that you will appreciate the benevolence of the Central Government and the importance of peaceful unification, and promptly come to Nanjing to take office, joining in the defense against foreign aggression. This is earnestly hoped for. If you still harbor resentment and pursue private separatist ambitions, disregarding the loss of national strength and undermining unification, then party discipline and national law will not tolerate those who harbor disloyalty to procrastinate in this manner. Moreover, the four hundred million compatriots of the nation will never forgive you rebellious individuals. The telegram is urgent. Please take heed. China Cultural Construction Association Shanghai Branch, Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Union, Shanghai University Student Union, Shanghai Middle School Faculty and Staff Union, Shanghai Middle School Student Union, Shanghai French Concession Private Primary and Secondary School Union, Shanghai Women's Advancement Association, Shanghai Youth Reading Club, China Labor Association, China Educational Film Association Shanghai Branch, China Scientific Movement Association Shanghai Branch, Newcomer Weekly, Cultural Construction Monthly, Times Newspaper, Yongjin Biweekly, Shanghai Farmer Monthly, China Postal Worker Monthly, Shanghai Social Education Society, China Boy Scouts Shanghai Municipal Council, Kuangliu Literary Society, Shanghai Cooperative Enterprise Promotion Association, National Reading Mutual Aid Society, Shanghai Unknown Writers Association, China Mental Research Association, and 56 other organizations respectfully submit."

Telegram to Lin and Chiang

"Respectfully submitted to Chairman Lin of the National Government and Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission in Guling. The recent unrest in Guangdong and Guangxi was initiated by Li Bai. According to party discipline and national law, he should be severely punished. The Central Government, considering his past contributions to the revolution, albeit with some merit, has already shown extreme leniency and tolerance by granting him the positions of Standing Committee Member of the Military Affairs Commission and Chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government. However, since the announcement of the new appointments, many days have passed, and Li Bai has not only failed to express frankness but is also mobilizing troops and concentrating them in Guangdong and Guangxi. According to reports, Li Bai not only intends to resist orders but also harbors the sinister plan to follow in the footsteps of the Red Bandits, fleeing to various provinces. He would rather sever the national lifeline and the people's lives than refrain from harming the people and the nation. This is abundantly clear. In addition to sending an urgent telegram to Li Bai, offering stern advice, this association respectfully requests that Your Excellencies issue strict orders as soon as possible, ensuring obedience to the Central Government and the completion of unification. If he persists in his obstinacy, then we implore you to prevent future troubles and eliminate evil completely by imposing strict sanctions. Otherwise, nurturing difficulties and indulging evil will be a grave mistake. The situation is urgent. Please take heed. China Cultural Construction Association Shanghai Branch, Shanghai University Faculty and Staff Union, and 56 other organizations respectfully submit."

Sichuanese in Shanghai Oppose Japan Establishing a Consulate in Chengdu, Write to Sichuan Fellow-Provincials Association to Fight for Sovereignty, Shanghai Student Association Forms Anti-Consulate Establishment Association 99

Japan's new appointment of Iwai as Consul-General in Chengdu has attracted national attention. The Sichuanese in Shanghai have risen up in opposition. The Sichuanese Student Association in Shanghai held a meeting a few days ago to study the Sino-Japanese treaty relationship and wrote to various Sichuanese organizations in Shanghai to send representatives to attend a joint meeting. It is reported that more than 30 Sichuanese in Shanghai, including Dai Yuebo and Li Jingxi, jointly wrote to the Sichuanese Fellow-Provincials Association, requesting that it convene a general meeting to make a strong statement. The original letter is found below (excerpt omitted): "Chengdu is not a treaty port, so there is no reason to establish a consulate. Moreover, the establishment of a consulate is the initial step towards extraterritoriality. How can we guarantee that there will be no disputes among the people if we allow the establishment of extraterritorial rights? If this happens, not only will our Sichuanese compatriots be subject to unpredictable influences, but the power of friendly nations will also penetrate the hinterland. Therefore, we have prepared a letter to express this to you, hoping that you will promptly convene a general meeting to express your protest and make a strong statement against the establishment of a consulate. This matter concerns the interests of our Sichuanese compatriots and the sovereignty of the nation. Your association should be happy to accept this request. Respectfully addressed to the Sichuanese Fellow-Provincials Association. It is also learned that the Sichuanese Student Association in Shanghai and other organizations have launched the Shanghai Sichuanese Anti-Consulate Establishment Joint Association and sent a letter to various Sichuanese organizations in Shanghai, saying: "Dear Sirs, Recently, it was reported that Japan will establish a consulate-general in Chengdu and appoint Iwai Eiichi, the head of the China Section of the Chinese Intelligence Department of the Embassy, as consul. Iwai is scheduled to take the Luoyang Maru to Chengdu on August 2, which is alarming. Chengdu is not a treaty port, and according to the treaty, consulates may not be established. The various countries in China have been peaceful for a long time, which shows that international law still exists. We are living in an era of national crisis, and our suffering has reached the extreme. How can we remain silent? Moreover, the freedom to establish consulates is not only related to national sovereignty but also closely related to the personal interests of all our Sichuanese compatriots, especially the direct impact on our Sichuanese businessmen. We are concerned about our hometown and should bear the responsibility for its survival. Therefore, we intend to launch the Shanghai Sichuanese Anti-Consulate Establishment Joint Association to jointly seek good policies to save the country. We urgently request that your association promptly send responsible representatives to our office at 5:00 PM on August 2 (Sunday) to discuss everything. (Rest omitted)."

Mr. Gao Mengdan's Treatment at Baolong Hospital: A Report to Relatives and Friends 100

Since my late father fell ill, he has been visited by concerned relatives and friends. They are also aware that his condition has been improving day by day, and that he would soon be discharged from the hospital. However, when they heard the news of his death, many were shocked and perplexed. They have been asking about the course of his treatment. I hereby present a detailed account as follows, hoping that you will carefully review it.

My late father fell ill on his return journey from Sichuan to Shanghai. Doctors diagnosed him with pneumonia. He was admitted to Baolong Hospital on June 29th and treated by Dr. Mertens and Dr. Li Mingchen. His pneumonia had been steadily improving, and his temperature and pulse were normal. His appetite was also good, but he often suffered from insomnia at night. On the evening of July 8th, he took two sleeping pills as prescribed by the doctor. From midnight until dawn, he was restless. On the evening of the 9th, he took two pills but still could not sleep. So, Dr. Li Mingchen prescribed two more pills. After taking them, he not only could not fall asleep, but he became even more restless, pacing and staggering. He closed his eyes and opened his mouth, unable to speak. He would sit up less than a minute after lying down and try to get out of bed. He used so much force that even two attendants could not restrain him. This continued until seven or eight o'clock the next morning. When Dr. Mertens and Dr. Li Mingchen came to the ward, they were told about what happened the previous night. Upon hearing that he had taken four sleeping pills, Dr. Mertens exclaimed, "too much, too much!" Afterwards, I privately asked Dr. Mertens about the harm of taking too much medication. He said that because of his age and weak heart, he should not have taken so many sleeping pills. Despite these two setbacks, he was able to recuperate through careful nursing, and his condition improved daily. His appetite also grew stronger. He was able to switch from liquids to finely ground rice, oatmeal, minced eggs, and diced wheat. Dr. Li Mingchen repeatedly told us that he would soon be discharged from the hospital. The family rejoiced, thinking that his condition would turn from danger to safety. Who knew that an unforeseen event would occur? Alas. On the evening of the 19th, my late father could not fall asleep for a long time. At 1:00 AM on the 20th, he felt restless and talked incessantly. At around 3:00 AM, Dr. Li Mingchen was called to examine him and prescribed two Evipan sleeping pills. Because of past experience, Junsan pleaded with Dr. Li not to use this medication and asked if it was possible to take only one pill. Dr. Li insisted that the medication was not as strong as the previous one, and there would be no problem taking it. After speaking, he crushed the pill himself and administered it with water. My father fell asleep immediately and began to snore. However, after less than ten minutes, he began tossing and turning again, sitting up and lying down, very restless. He closed his eyes and opened his mouth, as he had done the previous time, but with even more force. Even three people could not restrain him. At around 5:00 AM, Dr. Li came and injected him with Scopulamin, a sedative, but it was ineffective. Then he injected him with another sedative, Luminal. At the time, no one realized that it was also a sedative. He slept for less than two hours and then began to be restless again. He would get up and lie down, not resting for even a minute. Later, Dr. Mertens ordered an injection of Chloral hydrate, but it was also ineffective. The restlessness did not diminish throughout the day. However, Dr. Li said after each pulse check that his pulse was very good and that he would soon wake up. He also said that he only needed to rest for a few more days and he could be discharged from the hospital. At about 5:00 PM that afternoon, a Western nurse at the hospital examined his chest and exclaimed that he was poisoned by too many sedatives. She immediately called Dr. Mertens, but he claimed to be busy and did not come. That evening, Dr. Sun Dafang (Director of the Zhenru Forensic Institute) and Dr. Zheng Baoshi came to examine him. They were shocked by his condition and said that he was poisoned. They urgently requested Dr. Li to find a way to save him, but Dr. Li was busy with social engagements and did not arrive until much later. When he arrived, he still did not admit that it was caused by taking too many sedatives. The family had no recourse and brought him back from Baolong Hospital on the 21st. They immediately invited famous Shanghai doctors Huang Zhong, Zeng Yaozhong, Lu Jinwen, Zhou Zhenyu, Song Wusheng, Liang Junqing, Zheng Baoshi, Cai Hong, and German doctor Loewenberg to consult. All the doctors unanimously diagnosed him with poisoning from too many sedatives. Moreover, because the poisoning was too deep, treatment was very difficult. From 3:00 AM on the 20th to 0:05 AM on the 23rd, a total of 66 hours, the patient was never at peace for a moment. His suffering was heartbreaking to witness. However, the patient was delirious and did not say a word from beginning to end. When his strength was exhausted, he abandoned Junsan and others and passed away. Alas.

It should be noted that my late father had heart disease two years ago. Although he recovered, his heart was still weak. After entering Baolong Hospital, he was given a heart stimulant injection every three hours, which was stopped after many days. Then he was given oral heart stimulant medication. The hospital doctors were well aware of his weak heart. Why, then, did they repeatedly use large doses of sedatives? According to the doctors, the maximum dose of Evipan for an ordinary person is two tablets. Even an elderly person with a weak heart would only take this dose. In addition to this, he was given a sedative injection. How could this not be fatal? When we left the hospital, Dr. Li gave us a written report of all the medications used at the time. He omitted the Luminal injection that was given the second time. However, the attendants and the doctors who came to the hospital on the 20th had all seen the name of the medication written on the thermometer hanging on the door. The facts are clear. It is evident that the cause of death was the large dose of sedatives given the third time. Junsan and others were by his side and saw Dr. Li Mingchen administer a large dose of sedatives but did not know to stop him. This has caused an eternal regret. Now, I relate the course of treatment at Baolong Hospital, hoping that you will consider it with compassion.

Respectfully submitted by Gao Junsan, Junyuan, Jinxuan, Junzhen, Zhongqia, Shuge.

As for the former Consul-General in Shanghai, Ostovan, he will return to his country on a scheduled date after Mirsendeski arrives in Shanghai and takes over.

Gauss

Transaction of Salted and Dried Fish at the Fish Market 102

Effective August 1

The Shanghai Fish Market has decided to start trading salted and dried fish on August 1. All salted and dried fish shipped into the city must undergo the first transaction at the market, and fish merchants are hereby notified to comply. This market is an organization jointly run by the government and merchants to maintain and develop the fishing industry. Article 2 of the approved operating regulations states that the types of fish traded at the fish market are as follows: 1. Marine fish, 2. Freshwater fish, 3. Salted and dried fish, 4. Other aquatic products. The first transaction of the aforementioned fish entering Shanghai must be carried out at the fish market. This has been announced by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's Fisheries Order No. 416. Now, the ninth joint meeting of the managers and supervisors of this market has resolved to start trading salted and dried fish on August 1. From now on, all salted and dried fish shipped into this city must undergo the first transaction at this market. It is hoped that all fish merchants will comply with this order. For those who may not be aware, this announcement is hereby made.
