Tomita, Finance Officer of the Japanese Ministry of Finance, Arrives in Shanghai for Inspection 105

Japanese Banks to Host Welcome Banquet for Chinese Banking Community Tonight

To Proceed to Nanjing in Four to Five Days to Meet Authorities, Then to Hankou and Guangdong

Recently, the Japanese government and the private sector have sent officials to China in succession, one after another, to investigate various issues. The Ministry of Finance of that country has also dispatched Finance Officer Tomita Yutaro to China to investigate political and economic conditions. Tomita, along with four other people including Inamura Minoru, Ishizumi Shufu, and Takahashi Kouichi, left Tokyo on the 10th of this month. Passing through Korea, they traveled through Northeast China, Tianjin, Qingdao, and other places. They arrived in Shanghai on the Qingdao Maru of the Dalian Steamship Company from Qingdao on the afternoon of the day before yesterday and stayed at the Toyota Hotel, a Japanese hotel. At 7:00 PM that evening, they attended a banquet hosted by Japanese Ambassador Kawagoe, where they met with Wang Xiaolai, Chairman of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, and Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Xinliu, and others. Yesterday, they visited other Japanese officials and various Japanese commercial and banking circles. Yazuki Keiichi, the manager of the Yokohama Specie Bank, and other Japanese commercial banks in Shanghai hosted a banquet at the 63 Garden last night at 7:00 PM and invited members of the Chinese banking community to introduce them to Tomita and others. Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Xu Xinliu, Zhou Zuomin, Yu Qiaqing, Liu Hongsheng, and other major personnel from various banks were invited to attend. According to the Japanese Embassy, Tomita and others are scheduled to stay in Shanghai for four or five days. After meeting with various Chinese and Japanese banking circles in Shanghai, they will proceed to Nanjing to meet with Foreign Minister Zhang, Minister Wu, and others. Then, they will proceed to Hankou, then return to Shanghai for another week, and then go to Hong Kong and Guangdong. They will return to their country via Taiwan in the middle of next month. Tomita and others are tasked with understanding China's financial situation, and the results of their investigation will be reported to their Ministry of Finance to determine their financial policy towards China.

Xingyuan Steamer Telegram: Encountered a Maritime Accident; Shanghai Sends Telegram to Investigate and Report the Details of the Disaster 106

This office, Yongyuan Firm, received a telegram stating that the firm's Xingyuan steamer, carrying goods and passengers from Tianjin, Yantai, and other places to Yingkou, encountered an unexpected danger when entering Yingkou port. The ship suffered a maritime accident. Although the telegram did not provide detailed information about the nature of the accident, it only mentioned that the anchor was dropped at the time, but the anchor chain broke, and the large iron anchor sank to the bottom of the port. Based on this situation, it is possible that the ship was struck by wind and waves. Fortunately, the ship itself is still safe. After receiving the telegram, Shanghai, not knowing the details of the accident, telegraphed Yingkou, instructing the captain of the Xingyuan steamer to thoroughly investigate how the accident occurred and report the details as soon as possible. Currently, the loss of the anchor chain has caused considerable damage. The captain is instructed to find a way to purchase a new anchor chain locally so that the ship can depart as soon as possible to avoid prolonged delays.

Banks Participating in the Agricultural Credit Bureau Determine the Amount and Directors Yesterday; Six Million Yuan for This Year, Thirty Banks Participate and Elect Qian Xinzhi and Twelve Others as Directors, to Be Established After the Fixed Funds Are Allocated 107

The bureau initiated by Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang was launched in early May. Its articles of association were announced by the National Government on June 25. Now, after the fixed funds are allocated by the Ministry of Finance, it will be established immediately. Thirty banks in this city held a meeting yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM to determine the amount and directors. The result was a total of six million yuan per year, reaching thirty million yuan over five years. The amount for this year has already been confirmed separately, and twelve people, including Qian Xinzhi, were elected as directors representing the commercial shares, and five people, including Chen Guangfu, were elected as alternate directors. A report was immediately submitted to the Ministry of Industry for record, and a fixed banking syndicate will be organized to assume the responsibility of the banking sector internally, and the term of office for directors will be stipulated.

Thirty Banks Determine the Amount

After Minister Wu convened the banking sector for discussions twice, and after the banks voluntarily gathered and discussed, they allocated the funds according to one percent of the savings deposits. The first year's six million yuan has now been allocated by the thirty participating banks according to the second type of combined lending funds in Article 4 of the Agricultural Credit Bureau's organizational regulations, as follows: Four Banks Savings Society 840 (unit: thousands of yuan, same below), Bank of China 701, Bank of Communications 651, Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau 540, Jin Cheng Bank 518, Y盐业 Bank 497, Shanghai Bank 366, Jiangsu Farmers Bank 250, Jiangsu Bank 250, Dalu Bank 220, Zhejiang Industrial Bank 180, Zhongnan Bank 175, Siming Bank 150, Zhejiang Industrial Bank 123, Xinhua Bank 92, Tongshang Bank 70, Guohua Bank 65, China Industrial Bank 55, Guohuo Bank 46, Zhongfu Bank 35, Central Trust Bureau 30, Kenye Bank 26, Agricultural and Industrial Bank 21, China First Trust Company 21, China Farmers Bank 20, Agricultural and Commercial Bank 20, Quanguan Bank 13, Donglai Bank 10, Central Savings Society 10, Zhonghui Bank 5, totaling six million yuan.

Elected Directors Introduced Yesterday

In addition to the eleven directors already appointed by the Ministry of Industry, including the Minister of Industry, Minister of Railways, Minister of Communications, Secretary-General of the Economic Commission, Director of the Agricultural Department of the Ministry of Industry, Director of the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute, and Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau (the list has been seen in previous reports), each participating bank should nominate twelve people. Among the thirty participating banks, five banks, including the Bank of China, were nominated at the beginning of the week as conveners to handle the nomination and election affairs. Thirty-eight people were nominated from the participating banks as candidates for directors. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, at the Bankers Association Club on the fifth floor of Hong Kong Road, according to the combined lending funds, each ten thousand yuan of currency had one vote. More than twenty representatives attended. Qian Xinzhi was elected as chairman, and Wang Shaoxian and Qi Yunqing were the tellers. The results of the vote were as follows: Qian Xinzhi, Wu Zhenxiu, Zhang Peishen, Wu Xizhi, Zhou Zuomin, Wang Shixian, Zhao Dihua, Xu Xinliu, Hu Yun, Zou Bingwen, Wang Zhixin, and Ye Zhuotang were elected. The alternate directors were Wu Yunzhai, Chen Guangfu, Ye Xun, Li Fuxun, and Du Yuesheng, totaling twelve directors and five alternate directors.

Notify Each Bank to Submit to the Ministry for Record

The elected directors and alternate directors, as well as the number of votes obtained, will be reported to the Ministry of Industry by the conveners, representing the participating banks, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and the Four Banks, today or tomorrow for record. Each participating bank will also be notified that, for the convenience of mutual consultation, a fixed banking syndicate will be organized by the participating banks to stipulate the term of office for the directors and supervise the board of directors.

Convene a Board Meeting to Elect a Chairman

The twenty-three directors of the Agricultural Credit Bureau have now been fully introduced. A board meeting will be convened at the beginning of next month to elect a chairman. At that time, in order to promote early establishment, the following matters will also be reviewed and finalized: Business plan and regional implementation methods, Various preliminary and implementation sequences, Establishment of branches and instructors, etc.

Establishment Time Before Autumn Harvest

Currently, the funds allocated by each bank have been determined, and the fixed funds of six million yuan for this year can be allocated immediately. The purpose of establishing the Agricultural Credit Bureau is to streamline the circulation of agricultural products and agricultural funds, thereby seeking the development of rural areas nationwide. At this time when rural areas are gradually recovering, it is even more necessary to establish it as soon as possible. Therefore, it has been decided to establish it before the autumn harvest, and the date is expected to be in mid-to-late August.

General Manager Nominee Appointed by the Ministry

According to Article 16 of the Agricultural Credit Bureau's articles of association, the bureau will have one general manager and two deputy general managers, who will be selected and appointed by the Ministry of Industry from among the directors. According to the reporter of the East China News Agency, all parties favor Mr. Qian Xinzhi, the deputy manager of the Four Banks. Mr. Qian has served in the banking sector for twenty years and has a deep understanding of the hardships of the people. He is also familiar with the agricultural situation around the world and is the most knowledgeable person in the financial sector regarding agricultural matters. Therefore, his name is highly recommended for the position of general manager.

National Sugar Production and Sales Association Held Its Members' General Meeting Yesterday; Amended and Approved the Association's Organizational Charter, Telegraphed Mr. Feng to Come to Shanghai to Preside Over Everything 108

The China National Sugar Production and Sales Association, decided by the board of directors, held its first members' general meeting at the association's office at 129 Minguo Road yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. The association's charter was amended and approved, and Mr. Feng, the chairman of the board, was telegraphed to come to Shanghai to preside over the inaugural meeting. The following are the details learned by the Dagong News Agency reporter:

Members' General Meeting

The China National Sugar Production and Sales Association held its first members' general meeting at the association's office yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. The members who attended included Dong Junou, Zheng Yizhou, Yu Yizhai, Weng Pengnian, Feng Rui (representing Lin Qunyi), Tan Fu, Weng Fuyuan, Chen Xinfu, Lang Guangrui, and thirty-five others. Feng Rui was elected as chairman. After the formalities, the chairman reported on the preparations and then read the draft of the association's organizational charter, which was discussed item by item. Except for Article 21 of Chapter 8, which was temporarily reserved, the rest were amended and approved. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Charter Approved

The original text of the association's charter, as amended and approved by the members' general meeting, is recorded below: Chapter 1: General Provisions: This association is organized for the purpose of improving sugar quality, increasing sugar production, and promoting the sales of domestic sugar by domestic sugar producers and vendors of Chinese nationality. It is named the China National Sugar Production and Sales Association. The association's office is located in Shanghai, and branches or offices may be established in important sugar production and sales areas. Chapter 2: Objectives: The objectives of this association are to promote the development of domestic sugar production and increase sales efforts. Chapter 3: Association Affairs: The tasks of this association are as follows: A. This association may handle all tasks related to domestic sugar in order to complete its mission. B. Investigate the production and sales quantities of sugar in various countries around the world, as well as the planting and manufacturing methods. C. Compile national sugar production and sales statistics and try to regulate supply and demand. D. Be responsible for investigating the transportation of legitimate domestic sugar and issue certificates and guarantees to facilitate its transportation and sales. E. Guide and improve sugar production and manufacturing methods, and try to promote its sales. F. In order to support sugarcane farmers and manufacturers and producers, the association may provide relief if it deems necessary. G. Matters concerning the maintenance of state-owned and private sugar industries. H. Assist the government in inspecting imported and exported sugar under entrustment. I. Other methods to promote the development of domestic sugar. Chapter 4: Organization: Those who meet the following qualifications may become members of this association: A. Organized sugar industry groups. B. Sugar factories. C. Companies and firms engaged in the sugar business. Members in category A above are called group members, members in category B are called manufacturer members, and members in category C are called merchant members. The levels of each type of member are as follows: Group members: Class A may send one to three representatives, and Class B is limited to one representative. Manufacturer members: Class A may send one to two representatives, and Class B is limited to one representative. Merchant members may each send one representative. Anyone with one of the following circumstances may not be a representative: Those who have been deprived of their civil rights and have not yet had their rights restored. Those who have been declared bankrupt and have not yet had their rights restored. Those who are incapable of acting. When joining the association, members must fill out a membership application form, and when leaving the association, they must submit a written statement of reasons, both of which must be approved by the board of directors. Chapter 5: Rights and Obligations: Rights that members should enjoy in common: The categories in Article 4. The right to choose, to be elected, and to be impeached. The right to propose motions and vote. Obligations that members must fulfill: Abide by the articles of association and resolutions. Undertake the tasks assigned by the association. Pay membership fees. Respond to inquiries and investigations by the association. Not engage in any behavior that damages the reputation of the association. If any member or their representative violates any of the obligations in Article 11, they will be warned for minor violations, their rights will be suspended for moderate violations, and they will be expelled from the association for serious violations. However, if it concerns an individual representative, the member should be ordered to replace them. Chapter 6: Staff: This association shall have fifteen directors, eight of whom shall be elected from the production side and seven from the sales side, to jointly form the board of directors. One chairman and six executive directors shall be elected from among the directors. They shall serve on a voluntary basis for a term of three years and may be re-elected. This association shall have one director-general, a number of general affairs officers, and financial officers, who shall be appointed by the executive board of directors. This association shall have one to three supervisors to supervise the board of directors in handling association affairs. In addition to the chairman of the Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee serving as a supervisor ex officio, the rest shall be jointly invited by the members from impartial individuals with a reputation in relevant government agencies or the sugar industry, and then reported to the competent government agency for record. In order to gather wisdom and benefit from multiple sources, this association may invite people with a reputation in various fields and those with sugar industry experience to serve as advisors. Chapter 7: Powers: The board of directors shall be fully responsible for presiding over the association's strength. It shall exercise its powers in accordance with the provisions of this charter and the resolutions of the members' general meeting. The chairman of the board of directors shall be the chairman of meetings and the external representative, as well as the executor of association affairs. In the absence of the chairman, the executive director shall act on his behalf. The executive directors shall handle daily association affairs and assist the chairman in executing all association affairs. Chapter 8: Meetings: The meetings of this association shall be divided into members' general meetings, board meetings, and executive board meetings, which shall be divided into regular and special meetings. The members' general meeting shall be held once a year in August at the location of the association. The board meeting shall be held regularly every three months. The executive board meeting shall be held twice a month. Various special meetings may be convened when the executive board of directors deems it necessary, or when one-fifth of the members or two-fifths of the directors request it and there is a valid reason, they shall also be convened at any time. (Reserved) Chapter 9: Expenses: The expenses of this association shall be the following items: Annual membership fee of 100 yuan, annual fee for manufacturer members is 60 yuan, halved for Class B, and annual fee for merchant members is 24 yuan. Subsidies. Fundraising for special expenses. The income and expenditure of this association shall be reported in the form of a final account report at the annual members' general meeting. Chapter 10: Supplementary Provisions: The rules of procedure and various detailed rules of this association shall be determined separately. These articles of association shall be implemented upon approval by the members' general meeting and shall be submitted to the Sugar Transportation and Sales Management Committee for submission to the Ministry of Finance for approval and record. The same shall apply to amendments.

Telegraphed Mr. Feng

Since Mr. Feng Rui was elected as chairman of the board by the first board meeting, the association telegraphed Mr. Feng yesterday urging him to come to Shanghai soon to preside over everything, as the scheduled date of establishment on August 1st is approaching. At the same time, the progress of preparations will be reported to the Ministry of Finance for record.

Spring Cocoon Loan Syndicate to Conclude 110

The Shanghai silver and money industry organized a 25th-year spring cocoon collection loan syndicate to handle the collection of cocoon goods in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, totaling more than 10 million yuan. The term is three months, and it has now expired and is being returned one after another. There are still tens of thousands of yuan to be fully paid. The borrowers have contacted the syndicate and scheduled a date to pay off the debt within days. It is reported that the syndicate is scheduled to convene all participating banks and villages in the middle of next week to discuss the conclusion and report on the progress of the handling.

Various Banks Allocate Huge Sums to Handle Rural Lending; Banks Such as Bank of Communications Allocate 10 Million Yuan Each to Comply with the Provisions of the Savings Bank Law 111

Since the Savings Bank Law was promulgated and implemented by the government, it stipulates that savings banks must, in accordance with the provisions of Articles 7 and 8, provide mortgage loans to rural cooperatives and loans secured by agricultural products, which shall not be less than one-fifth of the total deposits. Although various banks have organized such organizations as the China Agricultural Loan Silver Round and the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Spring Cocoon Collection Loan Syndicate, or established special agricultural departments to handle various agricultural loans and guarantee the joint lending funds of the Agricultural Credit Bureau, the total amount is still often less than one-fifth of the savings bank law. Now, each bank has decided to invest one-fifth of the savings deposits in rural areas in order to comply with the Savings Bank Law. For example, Bank of Communications has savings deposits of more than 55,522,900 yuan and has decided to allocate more than 10 million yuan. Shanghai Bank has savings deposits of more than 36,574,000 yuan and has decided to allocate more than 7 million yuan. Jin Cheng Bank has savings deposits of more than 51,879,000 yuan and has decided to allocate more than 10 million yuan. Therefore, there is great hope for the revival of agriculture in our country.

Shanghai East and West Slum Dwellers Self-Set Slum Regulations and Submit to the Municipal Federation to Forward to the Public Works Department for Implementation 112

The slum dwellers in the East and West districts of Shanghai have specially formulated slum regulations in order to automatically restrict the increase of slums, carry out chain security, and promote sanitation and education. They have submitted them to the First Special District Citizens' Federation to forward to the Public Works Department for implementation. The regulations are recorded as follows: In order to restrict the increase of slums and maintain the existing survival, all the slum representatives should do their duties and help the Public Works Department to proceed and apply to the Public Works Department and the slum representatives to jointly form a powerful slum improvement association, so as to exercise it. Every ten households form a group, and there is one group leader. Ten groups promote one advance officer, and the officer is directly under the responsibility of the chief director's chain security. No matter the group leader, officer, or representative, if there is any improper action that damages the reputation of the whole and is counter-revolutionary, and is subject to criminal punishment, he shall not hold office, or be expelled. The chief director and the following specially set up five shares, one, general share, two, investigation share, three, sanitation share, four, executive share, five, supervision share. Each of the above shares is set up with two deputy shares. Except for office and expenses, no salary shall be paid. The annual expenses shall be 2 jiao (3/10 is exempted). This fund must be approved by the whole and kept by the officer. If the slum needs to be repaired or collapsed and wants to be rebuilt, it must first be approved by the local group leader, and the group leader shall report to the officer, and the officer shall declare the chief director, fill in the reason, and notify the nearby detective and public works personnel at the same time for supervision, so as to avoid arson and private fraud, otherwise it will be demolished as a private building. The ten households in this group will be demolished. Request the Public Works Department to issue a three-part household registration certificate, one to the slum, one to the improvement association, and one to the Public Works Department for reference. If the landlord builds houses or the road line reaches the slums and obstructs them, they will be demolished. If several civilian residential buildings are built, the slums will be unconditionally demolished in a number of households to avoid refugees. The society will pay a small amount of remuneration to the teachers and outstanding people in the slums to take charge of the night school. After the completion of the above items, those who need to handle them: 1. Consumer cooperatives, 2. Literacy class, 3. Charity, 4. Mutual aid business, so that the knowledge of the slum dwellers will increase and be introduced into the track, and will be reported separately when it is held. The association is not responsible for those who have not elected representatives or have responsible persons in charge of chain security. This slum notice will be carried out after the approval of the Light Industry Department.

International Trade Bureau Promotes Direct Trade 113

Assist Producers and Merchants

Send Letters Directly to the Bureau for Introduction

In order to promote direct trade, the International Trade Bureau of the Ministry of Industry is making every effort to assist producers and merchants to negotiate directly with foreign merchants, with a view to gradually increasing the experience of our merchants in direct foreign trade and reducing the malpractices caused by passive trade in the past. All domestic products are happy to help, so domestic and foreign import and export merchants have sent letters to the bureau, requesting introduction. Every week, the goods needed by foreign letters are published in the newspaper. Those who are interested in trading can directly contact the guidance office of the bureau for introduction. However, in order to implement the foundation for cultivating merchants to directly trade with foreign countries, the bureau is only responsible for introduction and guidance. The transaction conditions, payment, delivery, transportation, tax payment, etc. are all directly negotiated by the import and export merchants.

New Appointed Superintendent of Jianghai Customs, Zhu Changnian, to Take Office 114

Received an Appointment Order to Go to Lushan to Meet Kong Xiangxi

The Ministry of Finance has officially announced the superintendent of Jianghai Customs, who will be succeeded by Zhu Changnian, the current advisor to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Zhu is a native of Wu County, Jiangsu, and graduated from the University of Birmingham in the United Kingdom. After returning to China, he served as secretary and assistant in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, he served as the chief councilor of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. In the same year, he also served as the minister to Norway and Sweden. He went abroad in the winter of that year and also served as the minister to Finland in the 21st year. During his five years in office, he greatly promoted trade in Northern Europe. He returned to China in the summer of the 23rd year and was reassigned as an advisor to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Zhu is the long-awaited son-in-law of Tang Shaoyi, a member of the Central Committee.

Malignant Epidemic in Tongwen College Identified as True Bacillary Dysentery 117

According to the Japanese Shanghai Daily, the malignant epidemic in Tongwen College has caused great panic in the society. Yesterday and today, in order to eliminate this epidemic, specialists were recruited to devote all their efforts to studying the bacteria. On the one hand, the Shanghai Institute of Natural Sciences and the Health Section of the Public Works Department were relied upon to identify the source of the bacteria. Yesterday (29th), after research by all parties, it was determined to be "Komagome B bacteria", that is, true bacillary dysentery bacteria. It is found that this bacterium is more serious than "Komagome A bacteria".

Sluggish Business: Yongping Sold to Australian Merchants 118

Yuan An, Shun An, and Tongshang Ships Dismantled

Civil Aviation Industry Cooperates to Seek Development

Dazhen Shipping Company, located at No. 12, Bund, Shanghai, recently experienced sluggish business and internal problems. It suddenly sold the Yongping ship to Australian merchants. Other companies, such as Yuan An Company, dismantled old ships to reduce their burden. China's private shipping industry is facing competition from foreign businesses and is currently seeking ways to recover. The situation is as follows:

Dazhen's Yongping Ship Sold to Australian Merchants 119

Yongping and Yong'an, two ships of the Dazhen Shipping Company that operated on the Shanghai-Hai routes and specialized in carrying passengers and cargo, were affected by shipping competition and sluggish business over the years, resulting in considerable losses. The Yongping ship, with a gross tonnage of 1,421 tons and a net tonnage of 984 tons, has been sold to an Australian shipping company. The transaction has been completed. It is rumored that there are also some problems within the company's internal organization, but the exact situation is still under investigation.

Yuan An and Three Other Ships Dismantled 120

A reporter from Dagong News Agency learned from shipping authorities in this city that the Yuan'an ship of Yuan'an Company, with a gross tonnage of 1,794.95 tons and a net tonnage of 1,114 tons; the Shun'an ship of Shun'an Company, with a gross tonnage of 1,455.14 tons and a net tonnage of 1,071 tons; and the Tongshang ship of Tongshang Company, with an unspecified tonnage, were all dismantled at shipyards to avoid losses due to sluggish traffic on various routes.

Private Shipping Industry Seeks to Recover 121

Due to the laissez-faire policy of commercial treaties, foreign businesses have entered China unhindered, relying on their strong financial resources to seize the ocean shipping industry. China's state-owned and private shipping companies are under serious threat and are barely surviving. Since the Ministry of Communications convened the Civil Aviation Reorganization Conference, each company has sought to regenerate itself. Regardless of ocean, coastal, or Yangtze River routes, the cooperative system has been adopted to avoid competition within the industry. However, due to the decline of commerce, the shipping industry has not improved in terms of cargo transportation. The operating figures of various shipping companies are similar to those of the first half of the year, so it is not easy to recover from chronic illness in a short period of time. (Dagong News Agency)

Measurement Bureau Issues Notice: Changes in Xiamen Port Boundaries 123

Instructing the Navigation Industry to Pay Attention

The Shanghai Hydrographic Measurement Bureau issued Notice No. 179 regarding changes in the boundaries of the inner harbor of Xiamen Port, instructing the navigation industry to take note. The coordinates of the inner harbor of Xiamen Port are approximately 118 degrees 4 minutes East longitude and 24 degrees 27 minutes North latitude. The new boundaries of the inner harbor are defined as follows: The southern boundary extends from the eastern corner of Waijian Reef, drawing a straight line at 90 degrees to connect to the Xiamen coast. The northern boundary extends from the northern end of Zhoucangziwei, drawing a straight line to connect to the southern corner of Dayu Island. Then, from the northern corner of Dayu Island, a straight line is drawn to connect to the southern corner of Houyu Island. Finally, from the northeastern shore of Houyu Island, a straight line is drawn at 45 degrees to connect with a straight line drawn from a point 22 degrees 860 feet from the Xiamen Shipyard entrance at 315 degrees. Attachment: The oil tanker anchorage area is located between the southern boundary of the inner harbor and the quarantine anchorage. The location is marked with the words "Oil Tanker Anchorage."

Dredging Bureau Sends Notices to Ban Wood Rafts 130

Xing Zhigang, the chief of the fifth district of Shanghai County, requested dredging of the shallow beaches of the southern port of Shanghai and banning the stacking of wood rafts outside the dredging line to facilitate traffic. He received a reply from the Shanghai Dredging Bureau yesterday, stating: "We have received your letter of the 23rd of this month stating that wood rafts are piled up outside the dredging line in the area of the South Guild Hall public pier in the southern city, which hinders the berthing of ships and easily accumulates sediment. You request that the Public Security Bureau be notified to ban this and that a motorized ship be dispatched for dredging. We are constantly paying attention to this type of event. We have already sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to quickly ban this to emphasize river works. We are sending the original letter for your reference. As for the request to dredge the shallow beach outside the pier, our bureau will likely dispatch a motorized ship to dredge it by the end of this week. Please note." The Dredging Bureau also attached a public letter to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, stating: "We have received a letter from the Fifth District Office of Shanghai County stating that wood rafts are piled up outside the dredging line at the South Guild Hall pier in the southern city, hindering the berthing of ships. We request that your bureau be notified to take measures to ban this. According to the regulations of our bureau, wood rafts are only allowed to be temporarily berthed inside the line and may not be stored for a long time. Recently, due to negligence of the above regulations and failure to adhere to the boundaries, sediment has accumulated, endangering the river. It is necessary to quickly ban this. We are sending the original letter for your reference. We hope that you will instruct all timber merchants to adhere to the line set by our bureau and not to cross it to emphasize river works. Sincerely yours."

Flood-Stricken Areas Gradually Recovering: Relief Association to Close 132

Unfinished Business Transferred to the Relief Committee

Bank Advances Reimbursed by the Ministry of Finance

Last summer, Hubei, Shandong, Jiangsu, Hunan, Anhui, Jiangxi, Henan, and Hebei provinces suffered floods due to the Yellow River and Yangtze River overflowing. On August 8 of that year, the Shanghai Fundraising Relief Association for Flood Victims in Various Provinces was established to assist the government in handling relief matters. Nearly a year has passed since then. Emergency relief, agricultural relief, and other relief efforts in the disaster areas of various provinces have all been allocated and verified. The work relief project is still being carried out by the Relief Committee in collaboration with the National Economic Council and various water conservancy agencies. Now, Kong Xiangxi, the president of the Flood Relief Association, and Zhu Qinglan, the vice president, believe that the association's various relief works have been completed one after another, and the disaster areas have recovered, so the mission is declared complete. It was decided to close at the end of this month. The board of directors is currently supervising the internal affairs to speed up the closing. From the date of establishment to the present, all receipts and expenditures have been calculated and registered by the finance group, and other matters have been compiled into work reports by the general affairs, fundraising, relief, verification, and design groups, respectively, to prepare a comprehensive report and closing process to be submitted to the central relief agency for record. Unfinished business will be transferred to the Shanghai Office of the Relief Committee, and all files and documents will also be transferred to the Relief Committee for receipt. Internal staff at all levels will be transferred back to their original relief and charitable agencies. As for the 500,000 yuan of emergency relief advances that the association borrowed from the banking community in this city, 470,000 yuan have been repaid successively according to the contract, and the remaining 30,000 yuan are temporarily offset by work relief public bonds and have not yet been cleared. Now, this remaining debt has been transferred by the association to Chairman Zhu of the Relief Committee for submission to the 272nd regular meeting of the Executive Yuan on the 28th, and it has been approved that the entire amount will be reimbursed by the Ministry of Finance to the lending banks. Zhu will report everything to the Executive Yuan in Beijing after the association closes. Furthermore, various disaster-stricken provinces along the Yangtze River are now starting flood prevention work.

Silk Improvement Association Plans to Establish Joint Factory in Jiangsu and Zhejiang 134

The Silk Improvement Committee of the National Economic Council, having assessed the overseas sales of Chinese silk, determined that its position in the European and American markets had declined sharply in recent years due to the impact of the global economic downturn, and it was not until the second half of last year that it began to recover slightly. In the spring of this year, due to the sharp decline in Japanese silk production, China's international silk trade increased by a factor of two compared to previous years. Knowing that the association intends to organize a joint silk reeling factory in Jiangsu and Zhejiang to control production and improve silk quality in order to prevent exporters from manipulating the market and to promote sales, it recently decided at a regular meeting to send personnel to Zhenjiang, Hangzhou, and other places to consult with the Jiangsu and Zhejiang provincial construction departments on cooperative methods and to inspect the internal equipment of silk factories in various silk-producing areas. The negotiations have been completed and a report is being drafted to prepare for implementation. Regarding the total cost of ordering silk reeling machinery, it is planned to negotiate loans with the Agricultural Bank of China and other banks, using the purchased machinery as collateral. Negotiations are underway and are generally expected to be successful. In the future, the site of the joint silk reeling factory will be located in Shanghai for the sake of transportation convenience.

Chauffeur Drowsy, Driving into a Utility Pole, Causing Disaster 139

One Dead and Eight Injured Among Fishmongers; Driver Unharmed and Fled

A truck, license number 17147 and municipal license number 13119, belonging to Huifeng Trucking Company at 138 Wai Ma Lu, Nanshi, and rented to Tongshang Automobile Transportation Company at 20 Lane 998, West Huade Road, loaded with fresh goods and more than ten fishmongers, was driving on Yangshupu Road, Pudong, early yesterday morning around 3:00 AM, intending to go to the fish market for trading. Unexpectedly, when the truck reached the vicinity of Guangxin Road, the drowsy driver, Xia Zilong, did not turn the steering wheel and continued to drive straight, causing the truck to drive onto the sidewalk and crash into a wooden utility pole. Nine of the fishmongers on the truck were thrown out of the truck and fell to the ground, suffering serious injuries. The driver was unharmed, saw the accident he had caused, immediately got out of the truck, and fled. After being seen by passersby, the Yangshupu police station was notified, and the injured fishmongers Jia Abao (chest), Yu Santai (left foot), Jiang Xingji (leg), Zhang Qingsi (waist), Xu Bingsheng (head), Xiao Fazhu (hand), Ji Atao (abdomen), Zhou Jixing (mouth), and Nie Gongyu (head) were sent to the hospital for treatment. However, Jia Abao, 35 years old, from Pudong, died at around 7:00 AM yesterday because his liver was crushed. The escaped driver is currently being pursued by the police.

Conviction in the Case of Hobo Killing a Guard at the Hobo Work Training Center 140

Gao Fuxiang Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Hobo Gao Fuxiang, Pan Koushou, Hong Jianfu, and fugitive hobos Yao Benren, Gao Yongling, Wu Ruilin, and others, who were taken in by the Caohjing Hobo Work Training Center, dug a hole in their dormitory at night on June 2 of this year to plan an escape. They were seen by security guard Lu Yecai. They devised a plan to lure Lu in and beat him to death with iron tools. The training center's guards surrounded and arrested them. Except for Yao Benren, Gao Yongling, Wu Ruilin, and others who escaped, Gao Fuxiang, Pan Koushou, Hong Jianfu, and three other criminals were arrested and sent to the local court. The prosecutor filed charges of murder. After a clear review and final debate by the criminal court, Judge Zhao Yongzhou opened the court yesterday to pronounce the verdict: Gao Fuxiang was sentenced to life imprisonment for the crime of joint murder, with life deprivation of civil rights; Pan Koushou was sentenced to fifteen years in prison for the crime of joint murder, with deprivation of civil rights for ten years; Hong Jianfu was sentenced to three years in prison for aiding murder, as a warning. The ten criminals refused to accept the verdict. The court advised them to accept the verdict and appeal according to the law within ten days. They were then ordered to be taken back into custody.

Overview of Shanghai County Land Reorganization 141

Since the implementation of land registration in Shanghai County in May of last year, it has been actively carried out. However, a small number of property owners have not yet registered, so the deadline has been extended to August 15 to show consideration. The bureau yesterday sent a letter to various districts, instructing the heads of villages and towns to work hard to promote and urge registration. If there are further delays, the land will be sealed and investigated on a household basis. Furthermore, land ownership certificates have been issued in Beiqiao, the county seat, since the 15th of this month, for a period of one month. Various other villages and towns will also be issued on a scheduled basis. As for the land value tax, it has been decided to start this year. The urban and rural land value areas have also been divided. Rural land accounts for more than 254,102 mu, with an average land value of more than one hundred yuan per mu. Calculated at a 1% land value tax, each mu should be taxed one yuan, which is seven cents less than the original land tax of one yuan and eight cents per mu. The conversion of old mu to new mu is nine fen and two li per mu, which invisibly adds eight fen and five li to the current tax amount, for a total reduction of one jiao and five fen. Furthermore, urban land accounts for more than 6,300 mu. The land value of this item must be approved by the province. The county's field tax and county tax are collected in two installments of 40% and 60% each year. The budgeted amount for the 25th year is 110,234 yuan. It is reported that the land value tax is collected at one time.

Shen Yunqing Sentenced to Three Months for Embezzlement

Shen Yunqing, a local resident, 33 years old, residing at 26 Puqing Lane, Marang Road, French Concession, was in charge of selling stamps at the post office branch on Avenue Joffre (intersection of Avenue Mercier). Recently, due to debts owed to others, he was sued in court and released on bail with a deadline for repayment. Temporary Measures by the Municipal Council to Remedy the Shortage of Rickshaw Pullers 147

The Continental Daily reports that during the planting season, many rickshaw pullers in this port have returned to their hometowns to engage in farming, resulting in many idle rickshaws. Rickshaw owners are suffering considerable losses. The Municipal Council's rickshaw department has recently devised a method to remedy this situation, which is now being implemented. That is, rickshaw pullers who wish to return to their hometowns to farm can report to the licensing office and surrender their registration certificate. During their absence from Shanghai, the rickshaw owner can assign another person to pull their rickshaw. When the original rickshaw puller returns to Shanghai from his hometown, the registration certificate will be returned, and the name of the substitute rickshaw puller will be removed from the register. The rickshaw department's implementation of this new method is in response to a request from the rickshaw owners' association. Recently, a large number of unregistered rickshaw pullers have been arrested by the police for violating regulations. Therefore, the rickshaw owners' association petitioned the Municipal Council, stating that during this planting season, the number of rickshaw pullers returning to their hometowns to farm is indeed large. In order to maintain business, rickshaw owners have no choice but to use unregistered persons to pull their rickshaws and requested the Municipal Council to consider the difficulties of business and make appropriate accommodations. Therefore, the rickshaw department has this new method. According to a certain official of the rickshaw department yesterday, the Municipal Council's intention in issuing this is not to greatly increase the total number of rickshaw pullers in the Public Concession, but to facilitate rickshaw pullers returning to their hometowns for work and to prevent rickshaw owners from suffering losses due to a temporary lack of labor.

The Ta Mei Evening News reports that although the Municipal Council's rickshaw department has implemented a new method of substitute rickshaw pulling, 44 rickshaws were still arrested and sent to the First Special District Court on Wednesday morning for pulling rickshaws without registration certificates. Those arrested on Tuesday were mostly ordered to pay a fine of one yuan for release, and those without funds had their rickshaws held as collateral.

A Primary School Student Fooled into Mixing Counterfeit Money with Real Money and Secretly Carrying Red Pills, Questioned and Handed Over to His Mother to Take Back and Discipline 149

Wang Yongfu, a 14-year-old boy from Wuxi, residing at No. 25 Wuzhou Road, used a five-yuan counterfeit banknote from the Bank of Communications at 9:50 PM the previous evening to purchase goods at a cigarette and paper shop opened by Zhang Xiaoyin, a Ningbo native, at No. 499 Fielun Road. Zhang discovered the counterfeit money, leading to a dispute. Chinese Detective Chen Dabao arrived, and after questioning, arrested the boy. A package of 50 red pills was found on his person. He was taken to the Hongkou Police Station for detention. Yesterday, he was sent to the First Special District Court. Municipal Council lawyer Zhang Shizhu explained the case, stating that according to the boy's statement at the police station, he was fooled by someone named A Tu, and his mother was waiting in court. He requested a decision. Zhang Xiaoyin then testified about what happened. Detective Chen presented the counterfeit banknote and red pills for inspection. When questioned, Wang confessed that A Tu, who lived on Xikang Road, had given him the five-yuan Bank of Communications note and told him to go to the cigarette and paper shop to buy things. He was told that he could keep half of the change and would be treated to refreshments. He also asked him to carry the red pills, and he did not know he was committing a crime. His mother, Wang Wu, stated that Yongfu was her son, attending school, and had never broken the law. He was exploited by A Tu and requested that the court understand. Judge Zhong Qing lectured the boy and ordered him to be handed over to his mother to take back and discipline. The evidence was confiscated.

Two Prisoners Accused of Assaulting Guards, Hearing Concluded, Verdict on August 1 158

There are more than 300 prisoners detained in the Special Court No. 2 Detention Center on Rue Massenet in the French Concession. On the morning of the 7th of this month, a disturbance occurred because the prisoners demanded improved treatment. As a result, the French police were notified and sent detectives to stop it. More than ten prisoners were taken for questioning and sent back to the detention center the next day. Unexpectedly, two prisoners, Wu Sannan, prisoner No. 503, and Tang Jinsheng, prisoner No. 518, were injured again due to a dispute, with blood flowing from their heads. They reported to the Special Court No. 2 Prosecutor's Office that they had been beaten by the guards and requested an examination. Subsequently, Prosecutor Wang Ren opened a court to investigate and concluded that the two prisoners, Wu and Tang, had obstructed public duty and made false accusations. He then filed a public prosecution with the criminal court of the same court in accordance with the law. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Criminal Court President Wang Gangxu presided over the hearing in Criminal Court No. 2. Prosecutor Wang Ren appeared in court to state the grounds for the prosecution and requested that the case be handled in accordance with the law. Subsequently, Teng Guoxun, the director of the guards, testified that on the morning of the 8th of this month, the two prisoners, Wu and Tang, requested to change rooms. Because of my duties, I could not readily agree, and a dispute arose. The two defendants picked up slippers and a copper water dipper and beat me on the head. Liu Yan and Dai Rude, two guards, were blocking them, as testified by my colleagues Liu and Dai. The court ordered Liu and Dai to be questioned, and their testimony was consistent with Teng's. When questioned, the two prisoners, Wu and Tang, said that we were locked in the toilet room, which was small and unbearably hot and smelly. We had no choice but to request a change of room. Director Teng not only refused but also tied us with ropes and beat our heads with leather belts, causing us to bleed, and then pushed us into the room. How dare we prisoners beat the guards? There are layers of darkness in the detention center. Please investigate the court. If it is not improved and we are forced to live an inhuman life, please just execute us so we can be happy. Prisoner Tang also submitted a written statement accusing the detention center of darkness. The court verified the testimonies, ordered the debate to be opened, and then declared the conclusion, setting the date for the verdict on August 1. The two defendants were returned to the detention center. One bandit was captured on the spot.

Woman Divorces and Remarries, Again Meets the Wrong Person, Sweet Words Induce Her During Social Gatherings, Abandoned Not Long After Cohabitation - Gu Xuelin Accuses Hua Dafan - 161

Gu Xuelin, a 33-year-old woman from Suzhou, residing at No. 17 Houyuli, Old Garbage Bridge, recently hired lawyer Gu Yongquan and filed a complaint with the First Special Court against Hua Dafan (aka David), the director of the Yuchengfeng Candy Factory residing at Yongjili, North Zhejiang Road, for fraud, seduction, abandonment, and other charges. The reasons for her lawsuit are roughly as follows: The plaintiff was originally married to a Mr. Chen, residing in Suzhou, and had two sons and three daughters. The couple's relationship was quite harmonious. However, in August of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, she met the defendant through an introduction at a social gathering. He seduced her with sweet words, saying that his household was empty and there was no one to support him, and that he wanted to marry her. If she did not agree, he would rather die. She fell for his trick. Unexpectedly, her husband learned about it and reported it to the Public Security Bureau, who arrested him and sent him to the Shanghai District Court. Subsequently, both parties agreed to divorce, and the case was withdrawn. Before the plaintiff had a physical relationship with the defendant, the defendant personally wrote a note stating that if the plaintiff suffered any family changes due to the defendant, the defendant would be fully responsible and would marry her with the proper ceremony. The plaintiff then began cohabiting with the defendant in the 24th year of the Republic of China. On January 18 of last year, a formal cohabitation contract was re-established at lawyer Zhang Shijie's office. The content was roughly as follows: "Both parties will love each other to the end and will not change their minds halfway. The wedding will be held within one year. All of the plaintiff's expenses before the wedding will be borne by the defendant. At the time of the wedding, the defendant will pay a savings account of 4,000 yuan and 1,000 yuan in cash. If the contract is not fulfilled within the time limit, the defendant must compensate the plaintiff for a loss of 50,000 yuan. If one party regrets it, the other party may claim damages." Unexpectedly, after the plaintiff divorced her original husband, the defendant, having achieved his goal, disregarded his previous promises and moved the plaintiff east and west. Recently, because she repeatedly urged him to hold the wedding, the defendant became angry and abandoned her. This is clearly a crime under Articles 229 and 294 of the Criminal Code. A civil lawsuit is also attached, requesting that the defendant be ordered to pay 50,000 yuan. Yesterday morning, Judge Huang Risheng presided over the hearing in Criminal Court No. 8. The defendant did not arrive, but lawyer Wang Shouan arrived in court, stating that the defendant was currently in Suzhou and requesting a postponement. He briefly questioned the plaintiff, Gu Xuelin. The court ordered that the case be postponed and reheard at 11:00 AM on August 5.

Speaking of Worrying about the Times and Criticizing the World, Insulting Companions, a Ship's Cook Drowning and Dying in the River, Xu Abao Died Miserably from Excessive Anger After Falling into the Water 163

Xu Abao, a young man from Ningbo, 20 years old, worked as a low-level assistant for the Taikoo Shipping Company's Wenzhou steamer. He was a person who worried about the times and resented the world. On the afternoon of the 27th of this month, at 3 o'clock, the ship was loaded with coal to Shanghai and stopped at the Wusong Railway Wharf. Xu stood on the deck, leisurely gazing. At that time, a Japanese merchant ship, the Shanghai Maru, was entering the port. Everyone on the ship looked energetic and lively. Xu saw this energetic appearance and was filled with complaints again. He spoke in an impassioned tone, saying to his colleagues, "Look at how rich in innovation other countries are, making them powerful nations. As for our country, if there is no money at home, one immediately thinks about multiple wives." However, a chief steward, Tong Aqing, happened to be in a family situation with multiple women. He felt that this was intentionally sarcastic and subtle criticism. He slapped Xu Abao's face. Xu Abao was of a low status and was beaten and humiliated by Tong. He cried loudly. In the midst of his weeping, Xu Abao suddenly fell into the river, joining the water spirits, with no trace to be found. Tong Aqing took this opportunity to leave the ship and go ashore, with his whereabouts unknown, fleeing without a trace. Zhu Jifang, a foreign kitchen assistant of the ship, Dai Ayun, a second steward, Fan Hantang, a chief mate's assistant, Feng Chuanshan, a watchman, and Lu Gengen, a coppersmith, who were present at the scene, reported to the guards, who reported it to the water patrol police station. The arrest of Tong Aqing was unsuccessful. Investigators such as Xu Juelu were instructed to retrieve the body with the Wusong Lifesaving Bureau. It was recovered yesterday and taken to the Wusong beach. After Investigator Xu reported it to the local court, Xiao, the assigned prosecutor, and Yi, the examiner, etc., arrived at the scene for examination and confirmed that it was a drowning death. However, whether the deceased was pushed into the water or threw himself in due to humiliation and anger, the police department's investigation of witnesses was evasive. Therefore, the prosecutor ordered the body to be collected, waiting to summon witnesses for a detailed investigation of the facts, and ordered the arrest of the fugitive Tong Aqing to be brought to justice.

Letters to the Editor 167

To the Editor-in-Chief of Shen Bao, Respectfully, Regarding the matter of Mr. Liu Chunshan raising money on behalf of the parents of Mr. Pan Hongsheng on the Huaxing Radio Station last year, I handled it at that time and sent it to the Huaxing Radio Station for collection and transferred a fixed deposit and withdrawal savings passbook from the Hua An Bank to the Pan residence. The principal and interest of ten yuan in legal tender were withdrawn every six months, with a limit of ten years. Now, because the Hua An Bank is closing down all savings accounts and returning them to depositors, in addition to paying off the principal and interest of other depositors, it was found that the savings account for the parents' pension of Mr. Pan Hongsheng has not been withdrawn. Now, because the address of Mr. Pan is unknown, I hereby request that you publish a letter in your newspaper, asking the relatives and comrades of Mr. Pan to notify the parents of Mr. Pan to take the certificate and withdraw the money from the Hua An Bank and deposit it in another bank. This would be a great merit. Please publish it. Sincerely, Hu Gesheng, July 29, 1936.

Respectfully, I read the news column in your newspaper on the 28th of this month, which stated, "Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association Supports the Chen Case," and mentioned, "A temporary meeting was held at the West District Branch." I was very surprised after reading it. The association, apart from directly negotiating once on the day after the incident in the Chen Huizhang case, did not participate in any groups. As for the temporary meeting held at the West District Branch on the 27th of this month, no one borrowed the meeting place from the association beforehand. I believe there was no meeting held. I am afraid that people from all walks of life will not understand the truth and will cause misunderstandings. Therefore, I am especially writing to request your newspaper to make a correction. This is what I implore. To the Editor-in-Chief of Shen Bao, Sincerely, Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association, July 29th.

The Egg Industry in Shanghai (Continued) 169

— Chief Editor of China Credit

(Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Overview 33)

Traditional Egg Factories All are organized by Chinese merchants. One factory is established in Shanghai for manufacturing, and the rest are established in Jiangsu Province and other places in northern Jiangsu Province. The manufacturing methods are more advanced and can pay attention to improving quality. Some use hot air to dry. Among them, Flying Yellow Egg Products are manufactured by machines. Fuxing and Xinchang both have new-style machine equipment, so they are called new-style factories. The scope of each factory is quite large, with two to three hundred workers, and the capital is over 100,000 yuan. The list of traditional egg factories is as follows:

Export Companies There are no less than forty export egg companies in the city. In addition to Chinese merchants, British, German, French, Italian, American, Japanese, and Dutch merchants are all present. Most of them are transported to Europe and the United States, and a small number are transported to the South Seas Islands. This year, the German firm Lihé and the American firm Meizui have the most frequent sales. The list of export firms is as follows:

(Note: Maochang and six other companies are included in the ice egg factory category):

(1) Chinese Merchants Yingfeng, Huaxin, Jinhai, Futianshen, Yihua, Yuxingxiang, Judetai, Yian, Zhang Hongtai, Guangmaoxiang, Guangyuansheng, Guangyichang, Chengxin, Yuanshunxiang, Dongxingyuan.

(2) British Merchants Morse, Xinji, Anli, Fumo, Old Sassoon, Baoshun.

(3) German Merchants Meizui, Jiali, Chanshen, Lihé, Fulaide, Yali, Yitai.

(4) French Merchants Baiduo, Lixing, Xingcheng, Youyu.

(5) Italian Merchants Yixing, Xingli

(6) American Merchants Maosheng

(7) Japanese Merchants Kawauchi Kai, Zēngxìng, Kobayashi.

Egg Shops The business of egg shops is mainly based on selling retail and selling to small merchants. Fresh eggs, salted eggs, and preserved eggs are all sold. Most of them are operated in partnership, with capital ranging from several thousand yuan to 50,000 yuan. In the past, the egg industry in Shanghai was an ancillary business of salted fish shops. Gradually, the business became more prosperous and could be operated independently, and there were so-called egg shops. In recent years, the market has declined, and egg shops have closed down one after another due to poor business. There are Yida, Jiexing, Zheng Hengji, Tianzhu, Taishenxiang, Renchang, etc. The list of egg shops is as follows:

(1) Chinese Concession District Wanfeng, Jieshun, Fengmao, Liji, Yuchang, Chen Qingji, Zhentai, Lin, Xinchang, Tongxing, Tongmaosheng, Tongxinggong, Changtai, Xinji, Wang Xinji, Wang Songji, Hetai, Heda, Xintai, Yongfengde, Qiaxingde.

The Torch Passed Through the Hungarian Capital and Arrived in Austria, Vienna Prepares to Welcome It 172

National Maritime News Agency, Saigrad, 28th dispatch, The World Games torch passed through the border between Yugoslavia and Hungary at 6:00 this morning. A special ceremony was held in the town of Hargos near the border. The town had specially built an Olympic arcade, decorated with flower flags, which was very beautiful. Even at this early hour, there were 1,500 Hungarian cycling teams gathered to watch the ceremony.

After the representative of Yugoslavia delivered a brief congratulatory speech, the national flags of all countries were hoisted. The mayor of Saigrad represented Hungary in accepting the torch. The second torch journey was the capital of Hungary. 203 race walkers covered a distance of 160 kilometers.

National Maritime News Agency, Budapest, 28th dispatch, The World Games torch arrived in the suburbs of this city at 8:00 this evening. The race walkers were welcomed by the public, especially the crowds gathered at the Triumphal Arch. The Triumphal Arch is located in the center of the city and was specially built with a World Games torch altar and a viewing platform for officials and dignitaries. The Triumphal Arch was covered with lights. The reflection of these beautiful lights on the nearby lake was like the stars in the sky. The person who carried the torch to the Triumphal Arch in the Hungarian capital was Barsi, the Hungarian 400-meter star. Mr. Barsi hastily gave the torch to the mayor of the Hungarian capital. During the celebration, in addition to the Hungarian national anthem and the World Games song, Hungarian folk songs from all over the country were sung by the public.

Count Dulvivinberg, Chairman of the Hungarian Sports Association, gave a speech detailing the importance of the World Games. He said that the influence of the World Games on various countries in the world is becoming increasingly important. This influence is enough to increase international friendship and lasting peace. After the ceremony, the race walkers continued to depart towards the Austrian border, while the crowds at the Triumphal Arch dispersed until midnight due to the performance of the music team.

National Maritime News Agency, Vienna, 28th dispatch, The World Games torch will arrive at the border between Hungary and Austria at 2:30 AM on the 29th. Dr. Schmidt, Chairman of the Austrian World Games Committee, will personally light the torch and run the first 1,000 meters in Austria. The person who will run after Dr. Schmidt is Mr. Buna, Vice President of the Austrian Sports Association.

Vienna's preparations for welcoming the World Games torch are the most enthusiastic of all the places along the way. In addition to various celebrations, there will also be a lantern parade.

(Havas Agency, Berlin, 29th) The Olympic torch, which departed from Athens on the 20th of this month, has crossed the borders of Bulgaria and Hungary. At 2:30 PM today, it was passed to the Kidsey area on the Austrian border and will arrive in Vienna tonight. The German sports leader Chameosden sent a telegram to the Austrian Olympic Committee, expressing his congratulations and saying that "This torch is enough to symbolize the unity of the German and Austrian nations, and may it promote the lasting friendship between the two sides."

Accompanying the World Games Athletes (Part 4) 173

— Special Correspondent of the Central News Agency, Feng Youzhen

There are said to be more than 300 overseas Chinese in Colombo, but there is no organization. The most famous is Lin Baiquan. When our car passed his door, we saw a wooden sign with his name written on the wall. The driver told us that he was very famous locally. He has fourteen daughters and one son. But according to another driver, he has fourteen daughters and ten sons. He is a merchant who deals in safflower oil (a medicinal product similar to Mentholatum). He manufactures it locally and sells it in India, Singapore, Hong Kong, and Japan, and has accumulated some assets. He has lived in Colombo for more than 30 years and is now in his fifties. He is very kind and hospitable. Ma Dehan, Yu Hengzhi, Chen Deyi, Xu Minde, Liu Quanda, and others visited him. He knew that the food on the ship did not suit the Chinese palate, so he specially prepared a table of vegetables and invited them to have a full meal. According to him, only a dozen or so of the more than 300 overseas Chinese in Colombo are Cantonese (he himself is also Cantonese). The rest are mostly from Shandong. They used to come to sell silk. In recent years, they have been forced to wander in foreign lands and have had no choice but to switch to selling Japanese goods. When our car passed on the street, we also saw several Shandong merchants with packages on their backs, their clothes dirty and unbearable, and their appearance very embarrassed. It is conceivable that their lives are generally difficult. As for the shops of overseas Chinese, we only saw one named "China Commercial Company". The glass window displayed many embroidered goods, which were very clean and tidy. Because of the limited time, we did not go in to visit.

The climate in Colombo is similar to that in Singapore and is not very hot. The evening breeze is quite cool. We finished our tour and returned to the ship at 6:30 PM. It was already lit up with thousands of lights. At about 8:00 PM, we set sail again and continued to advance in the Indian Ocean.

(2) The Waves Became More Dangerous

The six hours of rest in Colombo gave everyone a chance to relax after the fatigue of sea travel, and they felt refreshed physically and mentally. However, after the mail ship left the port, it sailed again in the Indian Ocean. During these two days, there were often strong winds, and the waves lurking under the water were even more terrifying than the turbulent waves on the surface of the sea. The ship was constantly swaying up, down, left, and right, and more people became seasick.

The most painful thing for everyone was the unfamiliarity with the diet. On the one hand, it was due to seasickness, and on the other hand, the Western food really did not suit the Chinese taste. For these ten days, every meal was quenched with cold water and filled with bread, fish, and meat. Everyone had a great loss of appetite and regarded the dining room as a place to be feared.

Dozens of compatriots living in steerage ate Chinese food every meal. The ship hired a Ningbo cook to cook for them. When the players learned of this news, they were overjoyed and scrambled to ask him to cook Chinese food. As a result, the Ningbo cook did a great business. A bowl of fried rice with eggs was sold for 50 cents, and a meal of one meat, one vegetable, and one soup was sold for one yuan. Although it was a bit expensive, many people were still eager to relieve their hunger and there was an endless stream of people. This cook probably never dreamed that he could earn this extra money this time.

It has been two weeks since we left Shanghai, and everyone's hair has gradually grown. Some people tried it at the barber shop. Haircuts cost two shillings and sixpence (equivalent to two yuan and one corner in national currency), and shaving costs an additional two shillings. The barber no longer had any hope for the players.

It is 893 nautical miles from Colombo to Mumbai, and the ship needs to travel for more than 50 hours. It is expected to arrive at 6:00 tomorrow morning. The football team that is heading to Nanyang, India, will gather in Mumbai and go to Germany. The mail ship will have a 5-hour stop, and everyone can go ashore to relax again. However, there will be a 5-day journey from Mumbai to Marseille, and it will not be like now, sailing not far from the coast. Perhaps the waves at that time will be even more dangerous. Everyone is worried like this. (Sent from Mumbai on July 9)

Kant Float Terrace Wheel 178

(4) On the way from Colombo to Mumbai ——Our reporter Qian Yiqin——

After the ship arrived in Colombo at 1:00 PM on July 6th, the members organized themselves into teams to travel, usually in groups of five or six people, taking cars to view the scenery of Ceylon. The place has museums, zoos, temples, parks, etc. Although they are not very grand, they are all of a certain scale. At about 6:00 PM, the groups returned to the ship one after another, and the ship set sail straight for Mumbai that night at 8:00 PM.

After departing from Colombo, the wind and waves rose again. Many of the members suffered from seasickness and loss of appetite during these days, accounting for more than one-third, so various activities were invisibly suspended. However, the chess competition continued. In the finals, Wu Demao and Qian Yiqin fought five fierce battles, and the victory and defeat were not decided. Wu won the first game, the second game was a draw, Wu won the third game, the fourth game was a draw, and the fifth game was also a draw. Therefore, after the Arts and Entertainment Committee decided, the championship was divided equally, which was also an interesting event in the journey.

Because the food on the ship has been tasteless for a long time, some members have changed to Chinese dishes, but they need to pay extra, one national currency per meal, which is also considered expensive. The Western menu is roughly as follows, but it varies slightly every day:

(Lunch) Snacks—a small cup of light soup—macaroni—roast pork—fruit—coffee.

(Dinner) Vegetarian soup—beef—fish—ice cream—fruit—coffee.

Since the Arts and Entertainment Committee has ended the chess business, it has now launched a Go championship competition. Those who have signed up to participate include Li Zhou, Feng Youzhen, Hao Gengsheng, Wang Shoufang, etc. There will undoubtedly be fierce battles.

It is permissible to arrive in Mumbai at 6:00 AM on July 9th. Since departing from Shanghai, it has sailed 4,772 li, a total of fourteen days. It has now reached one-half of the entire journey. Our football players are all waiting in Mumbai. When the Float Terrace Wheel arrives, they will go to Germany together.

Education News

Measures for Enrolling Students in Employment Training Classes for Graduates of Junior College and Above – Deadline for Recommendations is the End of August 185

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 29th) The Ministry of Education announced the measures for enrolling students in employment training classes for graduates of junior colleges and above. Excerpts are as follows:

Measures for Enrolling Students in Employment Training Classes for Graduates of Junior Colleges and Above: (1) These measures are formulated in accordance with Article 5 of the outline for employment training classes for graduates of junior colleges and above. (2) Graduates of domestic junior colleges and above in the past three years (i.e., the 22nd, 23rd, and 24th years of the Republic) who have not yet found employment and who possess one of the following qualifications may apply for admission to the classes: (A) Graduates of domestic public and registered private junior colleges and above whose graduation qualifications have been approved by the Ministry of Education; (B) Graduates of foreign junior colleges and above recognized by the Ministry of Education whose graduation qualifications have been approved by the Ministry of Education and who have obtained a verification certificate. (3) Graduates who meet the qualifications in the preceding article and have not yet found employment shall be recommended by their original school if they graduated from a domestic junior college or above, and by the Ministry of Education if they graduated from a foreign junior college or above. Those currently holding any position shall not be selected. (4) When recommending students, schools shall be responsible for assessing whether the candidates have expressed opinions or taken actions in school that violate the Three Principles of the People or have engaged in other immoral behavior. (5) When recommending students, schools shall obtain the following documents: (A) A list of graduates requesting to participate in the employment training class (with format attached); (B) A graduation grade report; (C) A graduation certificate; (D) A guarantee (fill out and submit according to the attached form); (E) Three recent 4.5-inch half-length photos. The guarantee shall be signed and sealed by the guarantor. In addition to the school principal as the natural guarantor, there must be another guarantor with a proper occupation and a fixed address. (6) When recommending graduates from foreign junior colleges and above, the following documents shall be obtained: (A) A graduation certificate and a verification certificate from the Ministry of Education; (B) Academic achievement documents (such as transcripts, graduation theses, etc.); (C) A guarantee (fill out and submit according to the attached form); (D) Three recent 4.5-inch half-length photos. The guarantee shall be signed and sealed by two guarantors with proper occupations and fixed addresses. (7) The National Academic Work Advisory Office (at No. 2 Zeng Gong Ancestral Hall in the capital) shall be responsible for collecting and organizing the recommendation documents in Articles 5 and 6, which shall be submitted to the Preparatory Committee of the Employment Training Class through the Ministry of Education for review by the Review Committee. (8) Graduates who pass the review shall undergo a physical examination by the Preparatory Committee on a scheduled date. Those who pass the examination shall be admitted to the class for training. (9) The dates for the various procedures for enrolling students are as follows: (A) Recommendations: from now until the end of August; (B) Notification of passing the review: before September 16; (C) Physical examination: September 26 to 28; (D) Admission notification: September 30. (10) These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Preparatory Personnel of the Training Class Hold Meeting

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 29th) In order to prepare for the matters related to the University Graduates Employment Training Class, the Executive Yuan held a discussion meeting at the Ministry of Education at 2:00 PM on the 29th. Teng Gu, advisor of the Executive Yuan, Liu Zhendong, director of academic affairs of the Central Political School, and Lei Zhen, director of the Ministry of Education, attended the meeting. They had thorough discussions on the number of courses, the scope of the courses, the selection methods for employed students, and the detailed distribution standards for the 400,000 yuan in funding. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

Tai Shuangqiu Talks About Protecting Teachers 187

The Ministry of Education recently revised the regulations for elementary schools, adding articles on protecting teachers. The reporter, taking the protection of teachers' status as one of the three major goals of Teachers' Day, specially visited Mr. Tai Shuangqiu, the initiator of the program and the current Dean of the School of Education of Daxia University, to inquire about his opinions on protecting teachers. According to him, the current revision of the elementary school regulations by the Ministry of Education stipulates that teachers and staff shall not be dismissed due to changes in principals or competent educational administrative personnel. Teachers who are dismissed may state their reasons and submit them to the central educational organ for investigation and correction. This revision is of great significance. I also proposed a case for the protection of educators at the First National Education Conference in the 17th year of the Republic. Although it was passed, it has not been implemented. Today, the Ministry of Education has resolutely made this reform, which can be said to have opened a new era in the history of the Chinese teacher movement. All teachers should be celebrating. However, we should have further opinions and are willing to make suggestions to the Ministry of Education on behalf of the national education community, that is, regarding the dismissal of teachers, the authorities always have reasons. Except in special circumstances, they say it is either immoral or has no achievements. As for the so-called immorality or no achievements, it is only based on the subjective views of the authorities, and there are no objective standards or recognized norms that can be used as evidence. In this sense, protection is difficult to carry out as intended. In my humble opinion, after the laws and regulations protecting teachers are stipulated, the Ministry of Education should immediately convene education experts and practical workers in the education field to jointly discuss and determine the Ethical Codes for Teachers, so as to serve as a guideline for teachers to conduct themselves. Furthermore, various objective and precise teaching scales should be developed to serve as a basis for measuring teaching efficiency. After these two standards are determined, the status of teachers will not be decided by the personal interests of the authorities. When a dismissed teacher states the reasons to the competent educational authority and requests correction, the competent authority will also have a standard for judging right and wrong. I believe that the officials of the Ministry of Education have already considered this and hope that it will be realized as soon as possible. In addition, this kind of protection law should be extended to all educators. I sincerely hope that this item will also be added when the regulations for universities, middle schools, normal schools, and mass schools are revised in the future.
