Ministry of Education Actively Improving Secondary Vocational Education Nationwide 192

In order to actively improve secondary vocational education throughout the country, the Ministry of Education has ordered all vocational schools to set up school advisory committees and hire experts or leaders from the agricultural, industrial, and commercial sectors as committee members in order to make the training and education more practical and improve it. In addition, 850,000 yuan has been allocated in the central education budget, with 550,000 yuan to establish a National Model Secondary Vocational School to establish a foundation as a model for various provinces and cities, and 300,000 yuan as a subsidy for rewarding excellent secondary vocational schools. The former has been drafted by the Ministry of Education and the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund Board to establish a method for the Model Vocational School and has invited the Beijing Municipal Government to participate. It is reported that the plan has been approved. Basic subjects such as civil engineering, electrical engineering, and applied chemistry will be established first. A preparatory committee will be organized, and the municipal government will be consulted to select a school site. The latter was previously notified by the Ministry of Education to all provinces and cities to submit a report on the excellent secondary vocational schools in their respective provinces and cities by the end of July for review. Now that the deadline has expired, it is reported that the Ministry of Education will also organize a review committee to formulate review standards and carry out the review work.

Ministry of Education Investigates Overview of National Education Experimental Zones – Formulates Two Kinds of Report Outlines and Investigation Forms – Municipal Education Bureau Will Send Personnel to Investigate 193

In order to promote the experimental results of the education experimental zones, the Ministry of Education plans to compile a booklet of the general situation of the experimental zones in various provinces and cities for reference. Two types of materials were specially formulated: the report outline on the general situation of the experimental zone and the investigation form on the general situation of the social education, people's education, and rural education experimental zones, and distributed to the provinces and cities for investigation. The Municipal Education Bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate. There are the Huxi Minsheng Education Experimental Zone and the Gaoqiao Rural Education Improvement Zone in this city. The report outline and investigation items are listed below:

Report Outline: Report Outline on the General Situation of the Education Experimental Zone: (1) Purpose; (2) Origin; (3) Organizational System; (4) Main Business; (5) Talents and Funding; (6) Difficulties and Achievements; (7) Future Plans and Trends. It is clearly stated that: (1) A brief report on the general situation of the experimental zone should be compiled and described in accordance with the above outline, from the beginning to the end of June in the 25th year; (2) The number of words in the report form is limited to 5,000 to 7,000 words; (3) The report must be reported together with the investigation form.

Investigation Items: Investigation Items on the General Situation of Social, People's, and Rural Education in Various Provinces and Cities: (1) Name; (2) Date of Establishment; (3) Location; (4) Experimental Purpose; (5) General Situation of the Process; (6) Geographical Scope of the Experimental Zone; (7) Background of the Experimental Zone, including the number of people in the experimental zone, the number of illiterates in the experimental zone, the social conditions in the experimental zone, the poverty and wealth situation in the experimental zone, etc.; (8) Internal Situation of the Experimental Zone, including organizational system, equipment situation, staff, and funding; (9) Work, including work items, work purpose, experimental results, promotion methods, promotion effects, and any difficulties; (10) The host's opinion on the experimental work; (11) The attitude of the general public towards the experimental work; (12) Future plans and trends.

New Initiatives of Lida Academy 196

Jiangwan Lida Academy has complete facilities and strict training, and is a well-known secondary school in Shanghai. Eight years ago, it advocated labor production education, added a rural education department to the high school department, exempted tuition and accommodation fees, recruited children from farm families, and provided them with special training, aiming to train talents who specialize in rural careers to improve the countryside. The results are remarkable. The Ministry of Education highly praised it and gave it huge regular subsidies every year. It is reported that the school is planning to improve the rural education department. The department was originally located in Chaitang, a rural area six miles southwest of Nanxiang Station on the Jinghu Road. Now there is a Shanghai-Suzhou highway passing through it. Starting from the next academic year, first- and second-year students will be moved to the Jiangwan headquarters, and third-year students will remain in the original location. First- and second-year students will receive basic training, agricultural training, and military training. Third-year students will receive normal school training and rural service training. The Jiangwan headquarters has a large-scale planting field and livestock farm. Chaitang has a rural elementary school with many students, a farmer's clinic, and other facilities to assist the countryside. Graduates of this department can undertake all rural education work and are well-suited for the education, health, and sanitation work and the work of the Farm Bureau newly established by the Ministry of Industry. They are really useful in the national economic construction movement that is just beginning. As for the junior high school and the general department of the high school, they implement general education, which is no different from general middle schools, but the management is very serious. For example, in the graduation examination of this year, 19 third-year students in the general department of the high school participated, and only one student failed in physics and chemistry. Twenty-four third-year students in the junior high school participated, and only one student also failed in arithmetic. However, the scores of each subject in the examination and the school's usual scores must be combined at a ratio of six to four before graduation can be determined. As a result of the calculation, four high school students and five junior high school students each had one or two subjects failing and could not graduate immediately.

Yesterday, July 29th, was the settlement date for July futures on the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange. The total settlement amount was $19,001,000. From June 10th to June 24th, new low prices were seen. As the market price fell, buyers gradually emerged, and as the affairs in Guangdong and Guangxi shifted from tension to softening and eventually to resolution, the aftermath was easier to clean up after Chen Jitang fled. Short players in the market covered their positions one after another, and long players took the opportunity to add to their positions and raise prices, reversing the trend. Qingfeng factory's double fish Jiqing brand is selling at $7.50 for 9-pound, $9.40 for 13-pound, and $10.08 for 16-pound, compared to last year's prices of $5.06 for 9-pound, $7.06 for 13-pound, and $9.01 for 16-pound, an increase of $1.70 to $0.90 per piece. The factory's double fish Jiqing brand has been the most popular in sales for many years. Last year, due to higher prices, sales had already declined by more than half. Based on this year's sales prices, it is feared that sales will become even more sluggish.

Food: Japanese Merchants' Wheat; Futures Flour and Wheat Rebounded Together 208

After the opening of the flour market in the morning, the prices of each month rose together. The quoted price of foreign wheat, Chicago, continued to rise by $0.40, and Canada rose by $0.35, and so on. Market sentiment was stirred because foreign wheat had been rising for several days in a row. Moreover, Japanese merchants continued to export spot wheat, and although the amount was not large, it was ultimately considered an unusual event. Therefore, after the opening price, the near month was raised by one cent immediately, and the far month was raised by two to three cents. Later, because floating shorts continued to cover smoothly, there were no new short positions, and the factories did not hedge sell, so the asking price became tighter again. Compared to the previous day, the near month was better by one to two cents, and the far month was up by three to four cents. After observation, if spot sales are sluggish, it will not be overly profitable.

After the opening of the wheat market in the morning, the prices of each month rose together. The quoted price of foreign wheat also rose by $0.30, $0.40, and $0.05, and so on. The rumors in the market that Japanese merchants were buying spot wheat were heard in several cases. Although the total amount was not very large, the attention of both domestic and foreign players could not help but be drawn. However, in terms of quantity, it was said that it was only about 60,000 to 70,000 bags, which can be said to be insignificant. Therefore, to revive because of this is an overreaction. At the initial opening, it was immediately raised by 0.03 and 0.04, and then raised by 0.05 and 0.06. The price of November rose the most due to the largest amount of short covering, up by $0.10 alone, while the rest rose by 0.07, 0.08, and 0.09. The spot wheat market saw factory demand still not smooth, and the middle price remained unchanged. The special high-quality goods were raised by $0.04 and $0.05. Kai Yaowan and Suzhou wheat were at $4.56, and Mingguang and other high-quality wheat were at $4.60. Each factory went to more than 3,000 bags.

Indica Rice Is Still Being Sold at a Lower Price 209

Yesterday, the arrival of guest indica rice was still strong, and the source from the Yangtze River area was endless. Moreover, new rice from various routes continued to enter the market, and the production price became increasingly lower. However, guest processing was still strong, and Sichuan buyers were even more active. Yesterday, Shantou, Guangzhou, and Northern buyers, who had been silent for a long time, inquired. The rice market continued to maintain a strong position. However, cargo owners and hoarders were still eager to sell, and new arrivals were mostly sold at a lower price. Therefore, the hope of market recovery remained weak. Sichuan buyers purchased more than 4,000 bags of medium and final rice, Guangzhou buyers only purchased 200 bags of rough late rice, Shantou buyers purchased hundreds of bags of Xiangjing, and Northern buyers purchased a small amount of Guangdong machine rice. The rest were purchased by the local street. In total, 8,859 bags of Jiangxi rice, 1,200 bags of Hunan rice, 500 bags of Guangdong rice, and 48 bags of Wenzhou rice were traded in the unified market.

It Is Difficult to Reverse the Declining Trend of Food Rice 210

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, the sources from various buyers still only arrived at the 13th and 14th, with a total of 2,400 to 2,500 stone of goods. The local street sales market was still clear, and the Qingdao Dasi buyers only bought more than 500 bags, so it was still difficult to boost the market situation. The market for thin and thick rice was opening. The high-quality Zhenxian goods were stable, the medium-quality ones were depreciating by a few points, and the old and secondary ones were rarely inquired about. Duyang pointed rice was down by $0.05 to $0.06, and Yinbian Yuanhe had no goods and no market.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, 16 to 17 ships arrived from various buyers in Hexia, and the road for various goods on the market was very slow. High-quality white japonica rice was scarce on the market, and the price was flat and weak. The price of medium-quality rice was slightly lower by $0.06 to $0.07, early rice was scarce, and the price was firm. The price of thin rice was slightly higher by a few cents, the price of Yuanhe rice was flat, the price of various indica rice was firm for fresh and high-quality, and the middle and secondary ones were also seen to be becoming weak and soft. The price of the rest of the goods was peaceful.

North and South Goods: New Xu Kuizi Goods Have Arrived in Shanghai; -New Jin Cai Harvest, Weak Market- 211

New Jin Cai: Since the establishment of the company, the selling price has been able to be consistent, but the bottom price seems to be not very small. Now that there are abundant harvests everywhere, the market atmosphere is downstream, and it is inevitable that it will also be affected. Yesterday, it was heard that the company had opened up to the town buyers, opening up 200 packages of Daxingcai, etc., with prices ranging from 10 yuan to 17 or 18 yuan. In order to make the market price flat and straight, the company will sell it to the Guangdong buyers at the opened price without commission, in order to promote sales and make the price on the right track every day. Yesterday, more than 100 packages of Xuzhoucai arrived, the buyer called for 18 yuan, the company offered 17 yuan, and the transaction has not yet been completed. There is a soft falling image in the latter market.

Xu Kuizi: Yesterday, it was heard that a certain line rushed to handle several pieces, with a bright and dark color, and the identity of the film group was also impressive. The large line disk was at the 17 yuan level, but the number was very small and it was not enough to be regarded as a positive market.

Sugar Market: Hainan Red Rose Another Two Cents 212

The sugar market was stable yesterday. The association divided the market. The spot price of 24 coarse sand white was 21.88 yuan, the transit goods were 6.09 yuan to 0.08 yuan, and the 8th Holland red was slightly divided out at 16 yuan. The price of 8th TM mark of Dongbai transit goods was 6.5 yuan, which was 0.05 yuan lower. The price of 9th TM mark was 6.025 yuan, which was also 0.05 yuan lower. There was no upper or lower fluctuation for the rest. Ben Guang cotton white Zhen Ji and other No. 1 were still 20.5 yuan. The buyers in the buyer's goods tide continued to open more than 600 packages, and the higher price was 12.78 yuan, which was up another 0.02 yuan. Huayoubao was 12.06 yuan. Jianbang opened up more than 70 packages of Zhang red, with a price of 13.2 yuan to 12.2 yuan.

Yesterday, the joint company held the second tender for Cantonese coarse white this week. The quota was set at 8,237 packages, and the bidding price was the same as before. There were still few recipients. It was decided to sell 10 packages of Dongguan factory's five sheep group white for 21.7 yuan, and another 35 packages from Quxi factory for 21.03 yuan. The city's sand white was 50 packages, and the price was 19.02 yuan. There were few transactions. It was heard that Dundee factory's five sheep coarse white will continue to arrive. Its raw material is refined from Dutch sugar. The color and appearance are both excellent. It has been decided to sell it by tender next Monday.

Silk and Tea: Transactions in Local Factory Silk Are Not Smooth 213

Yesterday, the New York silk market was quite bullish, and Japanese silk and Chinese silk all rose by another 0.04. The current month's spot goods have not been auctioned. The selling price of the standard silk in the marun month was up by 0.035 compared to the previous sale. The prices of forward goods were also very high. The current spot goods in Yokohama continued to rise by 14 yuan to 18 yuan. However, the French silk market still showed no progress, and the prices of various silk products remained unchanged. Due to the sudden rise in overseas silk prices, Shanghai silk mills were even more determined to hold on to their prices. Moreover, this year there was a bumper harvest of summer silkworms in Zhejiang, and the autumn silkworms have not yet been determined to be abundant or scarce. Silkworm eggs are consistently viewed as high. Therefore, silk transactions were still not smooth yesterday.

Keemun Black Tea Sales to England are Recovering 214

The situation for Keemun and Ningzhou black teas in the Gengjin area is now stabilizing. Keemun black tea sales have already reached 50,000 boxes, Ningzhou tea sales have exceeded 8,000 boxes, and flower-scented tea sales have reached 15,000 boxes, accounting for eight-tenths of the total. Yesterday, Jardine Matheson, a British trading company, again purchased a large quantity, finalizing deals for more than 1,200 boxes at a price of forty-seven to forty-eight yuan, further stabilizing the market. As for green tea sales, they vary in smoothness. Needle, eyebrow, and pearl teas are selling well, but the most important category, "Zhen Mei" (Precious Eyebrow), has not seen any improvement.

According to a report from the Tea Trade Association, the tea market is still difficult to develop and transactions are scattered. Yesterday, Xiehe (協和) made a small number of deals for Zhen Mei tea at prices from one hundred and ten to one hundred and fifteen yuan, a decrease of five or six yuan compared to before. Ordinary Tunxi (屯溪) and Wuyuan (婺源) Zhen Mei teas continue to be purchased, with prices ranging from seventy-three to seventy-six yuan. There are also sporadic transactions in small needle eyebrow teas and shrimp eye teas, but the selling price is slightly weak. Only the Baishou (白頭) tea sold at the Gongxi (貢熙) market is active; high-grade teas are out of stock, and even the special Gongxi teas of medium grade are sold as soon as they arrive, with prices ranging from sixty to seventy yuan. There has been slight activity in large batches of Pingshui tea lately. Samsung, Kuaili, and Jingwei teas have all been transacted, but large boxes of tea are no longer in season.

Metals: East White Iron Market is Dull and Unremarkable 215

Since the establishment of the two Japanese factories, Zhongshan and Asia, in this port for East White Iron, goods from Osaka have been unable to come to Shanghai due to import taxes. (Because the cost of goods from Japan is twenty cents higher than the factory price here, the market has been eliminated in Shanghai). Therefore, the two factories here have been competing to ship goods, trying to sell them. The market price for standard sizes such as three by seven feet has dropped from one yuan and ten cents per sheet to one yuan, and the price for three by six feet has dropped from ninety cents to eighty-one or two cents. Although the price of thick white iron from foreign countries has recently soared (and the market here is also very brisk), the East White Iron market remains dull and unremarkable. This is because the two factories are fiercely competing, and buyers are fickle, so the market price cannot recover for the time being. There are few export transactions (due to the lack of permits), but sales within Shanghai are strong. It is estimated that the two factories ship an average of about 10,000 sheets per day, with more than 6,000 sheets sold in Shanghai. As for exports, they only amount to about 2,000 sheets.

The Issue of Qualifications for Elementary School Teachers 227

— Jian Ping

Recently, we have seen that education authorities, while rectifying and improving elementary school education, have paid special attention to the issue of qualifications for elementary school teachers: on the one hand, increasing the salaries of elementary school teachers and guaranteeing their tenure; on the other hand, starting with conducting qualification registration to restrict teaching qualifications, or rather, to raise the standard of teachers. At the same time, we have also seen the promulgation of the revised Elementary School Regulations. These regulations were revised based on the research results of educational institutions in various provinces and cities, and the experience of implementing elementary school education in various places. In these revised regulations, we have also seen the addition of issues related to elementary school teacher qualifications, such as appointment, treatment, and security. We find this very gratifying. The issue of elementary school teacher qualifications, which has always attracted attention, is now receiving such importance, although the results (methods) of this emphasis are not fully satisfactory, it is nevertheless a good phenomenon.

Elementary school education is the most fundamental education. In the stages of education, it is like the foundation of a building. It is the first step in education. Whether in training or cultivation, this is a very important stage. To cultivate good citizens, or to put it more plainly—to improve education, the first step must be to improve elementary school education. However, without being polite, our country's elementary school education is frankly and honestly corrupt. There is no need to mention the difficulties in the inland. Even in a large city like Shanghai, the corruption of elementary school education does not require any proof. Of course, the reasons for the corruption of elementary school education are multifaceted. Here, we will only take the issue of teacher qualifications as an example.

Most people have a mentality of aiming too high. The common general concept is that they often disdain the cause of education, very much like walking on the road of teaching is a sure way to starve to death. This is especially feared by elementary school teachers. However, we can say that this kind of person does not understand education. Although teaching is difficult, it is quite important, especially for elementary school teachers. Since elementary school is the beginning of education, if the teacher is not good, the bad influence will be irreversible. At the same time, the curriculum of elementary school is multifaceted, and the psychology of children is somewhat specially constructed. If one is not rich in common sense and does not have special research on children's psychology, one is not competent. Therefore, here we feel that: generally competent people who can become elementary school teachers do not take up teaching, this is the mistake of the general "climbing up" mentality. Therefore, the abuse of elementary school teachers has become one of the causes of the corruption of elementary school education.

However, we cannot blame them deeply. The main thing is still the issue of elementary school teacher salaries. Not long ago, we heard about a teacher in Xuzhou committing suicide on an empty stomach. As for salary arrears or lack of security, there are too many to count. It is especially terrible in Shanghai. An elementary school teacher is often worse off than a worker. Not to mention salary, even the food is not necessarily human treatment. This is correct. How can one teach on an empty stomach? Who is willing to be an elementary school teacher?

Now, teacher qualifications are restricted. Treatment, security, etc. are all stipulated in official documents. However, what we need is implementation, not just another piece of paper, a blank check to deceive the common people sitting on the cold bench to be happy.

The Face Reader's Trade 228

— You Qi

There, a bench was pulled over, and all sorts of people gathered to watch the spectacle, surrounding it in layers. The woman in the silk trousersuit had a face full of pockmarks, lips so thin they didn't reveal any red, but her eyes had an unusual gleam, rolling busily. The sunlight had devoured her fair skin, giving it the same glossy sheen as her clothes. And the one behind her? Silent, fanning a large palm-leaf fan, the breeze touching both of them – needless to say, that was her assistant.

Her hand opened, examining the crisscrossing lines, guessing the age, scrutinizing the features, rolling her eyes a few times. Following her usual method – take gold and jade hands and leave, your hand has lines of gold, no worries about clothes and food, treat people kindly and get no good in return. Just one pause, then, "What does your husband do?"

The woman's face flushed red, lowering her head. The people around snickered. Someone spoke up for her, "She's not married yet!"

"In terms of appearance, you should have good luck this year. Fifteen or sixteen years, your parents took care of it, twenty-something, you took care of it yourself. However, in August..." Her eyes rolled again, calculating the number, "You need to avoid three things: red foods, mirrors, and clothes drying in the sun. These can directly affect your good fortune – understand?"

"Understand," of course she understood. "Then – exactly which day?" the woman asked, convinced.

"The hour can't be known," her mind was laughing, the hour required careful consideration.

Needless to say, the face reading didn't involve "careful consideration," and careful consideration required a considerable price. Finally, she was disappointed, repeating the entire spiel, looking blankly, asking hesitantly, "Does anyone want their fortune told? Can you look at children's luck?"

"Why doesn't she look at her own?" I couldn't help but ask. "How much does this trade earn in a day?"

"She's a camel, pulling her along is the magic. As for earning a living? Unreliable, it all depends on luck."

She left, pressed by the demands of life. Fortune telling? Destiny? Why didn't she make her own destiny better? In the alley, different discussions were being held!

A Midsummer Night's Dream 229

— Xu Ji

The night was suffocatingly hot and humid, the sky was murky and dim, the atmosphere weighed heavily, pressing down on people, making it hard to breathe, as if harboring a great hatred and determination to crush these suffocating creatures into powder. Before going to sleep, people were anxious, exhausted like a pile of mud after a day of hard and hopeless work in the scorching fields. They often raised their heads, looking at the black, impossibly high sky, as if complaining about some unspeakable sorrow and misfortune. The sky was murky and black, clouds were moving heavily, as if about to rain or thunder. "I'm afraid a big thunderstorm is coming—why isn't it here yet? It's so hot, it's going to bake people to death!"

People all hoped for a terrible thunderstorm, so that perhaps it could moisten the land and wash it clean. Moreover, after the terrible thunderstorm, the weather would clear up, there would be a slight breeze in the fields, the sky would be azure blue, and small, bright and clear stars would twinkle in the sky...

However, the night had already deepened, and people were inheriting the terrible nightmares of their lives in sorrow, while the sky was still woodenly and silently dim. Inside the house, in the darkness, swarms of mosquitoes flew buzzing. Outside, in the not-so-distant pond, green mussels were calling out in a turbid, unclear voice...

Turning over, pulling at the tattered and dirty mat, in the swarm of buzzing mosquitoes, Granny Changlin, who was over sixty years old, burst into a loud cry again: "Oh, oh! What's going on! What kind of world is this becoming..." The terrible sleep-talking cry broke through the deathly silence of midnight, and Old Man Weilin, dozing on the couch, was also awakened. He frowned, and sighed heavily, as if forgiving someone. When he was fully awake, he resentfully and angrily rushed inside, grabbed the crying old woman by the hand, and shook her desperately: "You old thing! Wake up! Wake up! Are you going crazy again? Do you want to die!"

Tears streaming down her face, Granny Changlin was awakened from a terrible nightmare she had never had before. A surge of anger and sorrow constantly surged in her aging brain, and sobs and whimpers turned her hoarse voice into a string of disjointed, primitive sounds. But, even with so much effort, she finally used all her courage and difficulty to describe some terrible things: "I dreamed of our Changlin... covered in blood... he was killed by ×× people, like killing a pig..."

It's like a stone sinking into the sea when a person is gone. It's been half a month, and there's still no news at all. Who knows where he's lost in the world?

However, finally thinking of a great solution, with a begging tone, Granny Changlin said to her "old man" again: "Tomorrow, you go to the street to inquire again..."

"Go to sleep! Where to inquire?"

She didn't have the courage to continue speaking. The old man lay down on the broken bed, sighed, and his moist, presbyopic eyes looked straight out from the night sky: everything was dark. Mosquitoes were flying and calling. Frogs were croaking in the nearby pond. The sky was black, the atmosphere was heavy and suffocating, and the hot air was steaming like fog. There wasn't even a hint of wind around...

Old Man Changlin suddenly paused for a moment, and a painful, bone-chilling sting rushed out from the bottom of his heart, trampling on him fiercely! But he finally endured it, as if harboring an even greater resentment, changed to a slightly rough tone, and said in a low voice: "Don't go so crazy! How could such a thing happen...? Don't shout and scream like that. There's a curfew outside today, and there are sentries nearby. It's not a joke if they hear it..."

"What's the big deal? At most, it's just dying. Being over sixty, I still have to suffer that kind of torment, watching my son being caught, for so long, not knowing if he's dead or alive! What's the point of me living? Let me die, let them come and arrest me!"

However, even though she said that, at the thought of the gun butts and bayonets of those robber-like soldiers, she unconsciously lowered her voice. Such a strong man of thirty-six! Changlin, pulling a rickshaw on the street, argued with those "devil" soldiers over not paying the rickshaw fare, got drunk in a small tavern at night, and then babbled and nagged for a while, scolding and scolding, and was caught by detectives...

Sailor 230

— Meng Hua

The tide has come, we have untied the ropes, and with the full sails, we are at sea.

Our masts are spinning seven-colored bright lights. On the azure sea, under the moonlight, the sparse boats in the distance are swaying, the white sails like a dream.

Accompanied by the roaring sound of the waves, we sang. The low-flying seabirds shook their wings and applauded us. We are the gypsies of the sea, last year we spent early autumn on the Mediterranean coast, stroking the withered yellow grape leaves, chasing after our motherland, now it is summer, we are leaving the country again, gradually getting farther and farther away. The eyes that were hoping have withered, only the singing voice is still the same as in previous years. We sing, for the sea, for our melancholy, I sing endlessly. We love the sea, the sea is our relative, but no one in the world knows the sea in our hearts!

Dreams are lost in the vast waves. In the sound of the waves, I smell the fragrance of orange blossoms from my hometown, and I also see my mother's hair as silky, white, white. Like the silver light on the sea waves. And what about our hope?

The night is getting darker, the constellations are whispering, and the edges are revealing some secrets. The never-blinking waves, like our relatives, are always gazing at us, but our relatives are gradually getting farther and farther away.

How can I stop the dark shadows of memory from returning to my heart? When will the misfortunes of many years be relieved? Like a consumptive woman looking forward to her tomorrow, but by tomorrow her singing voice will have already become hoarse. Youth is like a illusory hope, like a strand of silk, blown away by the wind from beyond the sky.

Only the sea sounds endlessly melancholic, accompanying our songs. Now the sea is also dim, and I am also sobbing, because we have left our hometown, if the orchard is already far away.

Tanci (a type of Chinese musical storytelling) 231

Qian Jingzhang, Qian Zuixian, Mao Family Books

Sino-Western (1040) 10:00 AM to 10:45 AM

Opening piece: One of the Twenty-Four Filial Exemplars, "Zeng Shen Bites His Finger to Feel His Mother's Pain"

In a remote and desolate small village. Fishermen, woodcutters, farmers, and scholars fill the town. Hermits often emerge from deep in the mountains. Living a life of leisure behind wattle doors and thatched gates. Mostly carefree and leisurely people. Composing poetry under the moonlight, secretly lamenting their fate. There is a handsome young woodcutter. He is the filial Zeng Shen, carrying firewood into the mountains. He studies Confucian teachings under the tutelage of a master. He is extremely filial to his mother. Everyone in the village knows that he is a filial son. His good reputation has spread throughout the town. One day, Zeng Shen went into the mountains with an axe. To chop wood and buy rice for his dear mother. Unexpectedly, a guest arrived at the house. Zeng's mother was at a loss on how to entertain the guest. Being shy and lacking resources. With no wine, food, or money. She waited anxiously for her son to return, but he was nowhere to be seen. Knowing that the mother and son were connected by blood. Their spirits were intertwined and responsive to each other. She bit her finger with a hard heart. Zeng Shen felt pain in his heart.

Commentary

The Qualification Problem of Elementary School Teachers 232

— Jianping

Recently, we have seen that the education authorities, in the rectification and improvement of elementary school education, have paid special attention to the issue of the qualifications of elementary school teachers. On the one hand, they are improving the treatment of elementary school teachers and guaranteeing their tenure. On the other hand, they are starting with the organization of certification and registration to restrict the qualifications of teachers, or rather, to raise the standards for teachers. At the same time, we have also seen the promulgation of the revised elementary school regulations, which are based on the research results of education authorities in various provinces and cities, and the experience of implementing elementary school education in various places. In these revised regulations, we have also seen the special addition of issues related to the qualifications of elementary school teachers, such as appointment, treatment, guarantee, and so on. We feel that this is very gratifying. The issue of the qualifications of elementary school teachers, which has always attracted attention, is now receiving such attention. Although the results (methods) of this attention are not fully satisfactory, it is not necessarily a bad phenomenon.

Elementary school education is the most fundamental education. In the stage of education, it is like the foundation of a building, the first step in education. Whether in training or cultivation, this is a very important stage. To cultivate good people, or to put it more clearly—to improve education, the first step is to improve elementary school education. However, to be frank, elementary school education in our country is terribly corrupt. Leaving aside the interior, which is limited by various difficulties, even in Shanghai, this big city, the corruption of elementary school education really does not need much evidence. Of course, there are many reasons why elementary school education is corrupt. Here, we will only take the issue of teacher qualifications as an example.

Generally speaking, people have a psychology of aiming high. The common general concept is often dismissive of the education industry, as if embarking on the path of teaching is undoubtedly a path to starvation, especially for elementary school teachers. However, we can say that this kind of person does not understand education. Although teaching is hard, it is quite important, and especially so for elementary school teachers. Since elementary school is the beginning of education, if the teachers are not good, the negative impact will be irreparable. At the same time, the curriculum of elementary schools is multifaceted, and the psychology of children is somewhat specially structured. If one is not rich in common sense and does not have special research on child psychology, one is not competent. Therefore, here we feel that the failure of generally qualified elementary school teachers to teach is an error of the general "climbing up" psychology. As a result, the corruption and abuse of elementary school teachers has become one of the reasons for the current corruption of elementary school education.

However, we cannot completely blame them. The main issue is still the treatment of elementary school teachers. Not long ago, we heard about a teacher in Xuzhou committing suicide from starvation. As for arrears in salary, or the lack of security, there are too many to count. In Shanghai, it is even more terrible. An elementary school teacher is often worse off than a worker. Not to mention the salary, even the food is not necessarily the treatment of a human being. That's right, how can you teach when you are hungry? Who would want to be an elementary school teacher?

Now the qualifications of teachers are restricted. Treatment, guarantee, etc. are all stipulated in official documents. However, what we need is implementation, not just another piece of paper, a blank check to deceive the common people sitting on the cold bench into being happy.

Face Reading 233

— You Qi

Here, the stool was pulled over, and all kinds of people seemed to be watching a special spectacle, surrounding them in layers. The woman wearing silk trousers and a silk jacket, with a face full of pockmarks, and lips so thin that no red could be seen, but eyes with an unusual brilliance, rolling around. The sunlight had devoured her fair skin, which, like her clothes, had a layer of bright light. What about the one behind? Not saying a word. Waving a banana leaf fan, the wind hitting the two of them, needless to say, that was an assistant.

Spreading out her hand, she looked at the crisscrossing lines, guessed at her age, and carefully examined her facial features, rolling her eyes a few times, according to her usual secret—a golden hand and a jade hand, take it and go, your hand, the lines are intertwined into gold, you don't have to worry about wearing and using, treat people kindly, but don't get good rewards. She paused for a moment, and asked, what does your husband do?

The woman's face turned red, and she lowered her head. The people around were snickering. Someone, not knowing who, said on her behalf: "She's not married yet!"

—In terms of appearance, you should have happy events this year. Your parents cultivated virtue when you were fifteen or sixteen, and you cultivated virtue yourself when you were in your early twenties. However, in August—her eyes rolled again, calculating the number in her mind, there are three things to avoid: you can't eat red things, you can't look in the mirror, and you can't dry your clothes in the sun. These can have a direct impact on your destiny with a good match—understand?

Of course, she understood. Then—what day is it exactly? The woman believed it and asked.

—I don't know the hour. She was smiling in her heart. The hour needs to be deduced to be known.

Needless to say, face reading does not involve "deduction." To deduce, there must be a considerable price. Finally, she was disappointed, smashed everything completely, opened her dazed eyes, and asked tentatively: Does anyone want to have their face read? Do you read children's faces?

—Why doesn't that one read faces? I couldn't help but ask: How much do you earn a day doing this?

—She is a camel, it only works if you lead her. Earning a living? Unreliable, it depends entirely on luck.

They left, their hearts tightly bitten by the needs of life. Face reading? Destiny? Why doesn't she make her own destiny better? Those left in the alley were having different discussions!

A Midsummer Night's Dream 234

— Xu Ji

The night was suffocatingly hot and humid, the sky was murky and dim, the atmosphere weighed heavily, pressing down on people, making it hard to breathe, as if harboring a great hatred and determination to crush these suffocating creatures into powder. Before going to sleep, people were anxious, exhausted like a pile of mud after a day of hard and hopeless work in the scorching fields. They often raised their heads, looking at the black, impossibly high sky, as if complaining about some unspeakable sorrow and misfortune. The sky was murky and black, clouds were moving heavily, as if about to rain or thunder. "I'm afraid a big thunderstorm is coming—why isn't it here yet? It's so hot, it's going to bake people to death!"

People all hoped for a terrible thunderstorm, so that perhaps it could moisten the land and wash it clean. Moreover, after the terrible thunderstorm, the weather would clear up, there would be a slight breeze in the fields, the sky would be azure blue, and small, bright and clear stars would twinkle in the sky...

However, the night had already deepened, and people were inheriting the terrible nightmares of their lives in sorrow, while the sky was still woodenly and silently dim. Inside the house, in the darkness, swarms of mosquitoes flew buzzing. Outside, in the not-so-distant pond, green mussels were calling out in a turbid, unclear voice...

Turning over, pulling at the tattered and dirty mat, in the swarm of buzzing mosquitoes, Granny Changlin, who was over sixty years old, burst into a loud cry again: "Oh, oh! What's going on! What kind of world is this becoming..." The terrible sleep-talking cry broke through the deathly silence of midnight, and Old Man Weilin, dozing on the couch, was also awakened. He frowned, and sighed heavily, as if forgiving someone. When he was fully awake, he resentfully and angrily rushed inside, grabbed the crying old woman by the hand, and shook her desperately: "You old thing! Wake up! Wake up! Are you going crazy again? Do you want to die!"

Tears streaming down her face, Granny Changlin was awakened from a terrible nightmare she had never had before. A surge of anger and sorrow constantly surged in her aging brain, and sobs and whimpers turned her hoarse voice into a string of disjointed, primitive sounds. But, even with so much effort, she finally used all her courage and difficulty to describe some terrible things: "I dreamed of our Changlin... covered in blood... he was killed by ×× people, like killing a pig..."

It's like a stone sinking into the sea when a person is gone. It's been half a month, and there's still no news at all. Who knows where he's lost in the world?

However, finally thinking of a great solution, with a begging tone, Granny Changlin said to her "old man" again: "Tomorrow, you go to the street to inquire again..."

"Go to sleep! Where to inquire?"

She didn't have the courage to continue speaking. The old man lay down on the broken bed, sighed, and his moist, presbyopic eyes looked straight out from the night sky: everything was dark. Mosquitoes were flying and calling. Frogs were croaking in the nearby pond. The sky was black, the atmosphere was heavy and suffocating, and the hot air was steaming like fog. There wasn't even a hint of wind around...

Old Man Changlin suddenly paused for a moment, and a painful, bone-chilling sting rushed out from the bottom of his heart, trampling on him fiercely! But he finally endured it, as if harboring an even greater resentment, changed to a slightly rough tone, and said in a low voice: "Don't go so crazy! How could such a thing happen...? Don't shout and scream like that. There's a curfew outside today, and there are sentries nearby. It's not a joke if they hear it..."

"What's the big deal? At most, it's just dying. Being over sixty, I still have to suffer that kind of torment, watching my son being caught, for so long, not knowing if he's dead or alive! What's the point of me living? Let me die, let them come and arrest me!"

However, even though she said that, at the thought of the gun butts and bayonets of those robber-like soldiers, she unconsciously lowered her voice. Such a strong man of thirty-six! Changlin, pulling a rickshaw on the street, argued with those "devil" soldiers over not paying the rickshaw fare, got drunk in a small tavern at night, and then babbled and nagged for a while, scolding and scolding, and was caught by detectives...

Sailor 235

— Meng Hua

The tide has come, we have untied the ropes, and with the full sails, we are at sea.

Our masts are spinning seven-colored bright lights. On the azure sea, under the moonlight, the sparse boats in the distance are swaying, the white sails like a dream.

Accompanied by the roaring sound of the waves, we sang. The low-flying seabirds shook their wings and applauded us. We are the gypsies of the sea, last year we spent early autumn on the Mediterranean coast, stroking the withered yellow grape leaves, chasing after our motherland, now it is summer, we are leaving the country again, gradually getting farther and farther away. The eyes that were hoping have withered, only the singing voice is still the same as in previous years. We sing, for the sea, for our melancholy, I sing endlessly. We love the sea, the sea is our relative, but no one in the world knows the sea in our hearts!

Dreams are lost in the vast waves. In the sound of the waves, I smell the fragrance of orange blossoms from my hometown, and I also see my mother's hair as silky, white, white. Like the silver light on the sea waves. And what about our hope?

The night is getting darker, the constellations are whispering, and the edges are revealing some secrets. The never-blinking waves, like our relatives, are always gazing at us, but our relatives are gradually getting farther and farther away.

How can I stop the dark shadows of memory from returning to my heart? When will the misfortunes of many years be relieved? Like a consumptive woman looking forward to her tomorrow, but by tomorrow her singing voice will have already become hoarse. Youth is like a illusory hope, like a strand of silk, blown away by the wind from beyond the sky.

Only the sea sounds endlessly melancholic, accompanying our songs. Now the sea is also dim, and I am also sobbing, because we have left our hometown, if the orchard is already far away.

Storytelling 236

Qian Jingzhang, Qian Zuixian, Mao Family Book

Zhongxi (1040) 10:00 AM to 10:45 AM

Opening chapter: One of the Twenty-Four Filial Exemplars, "Zeng Shen Bites His Finger and Feels the Pain" – A secluded and desolate little village. Fishermen, woodcutters, farmers, and scholars fill the town. Hermits often emerge from the deep mountains. Thatched gates and wattle doors pass the days. Most of them are detached and leisurely people. They secretly grieve while reciting poetry under the moon. There is a handsome and brave young firewood cutter. He is actually Zeng Shen, a virtuous man who carries firewood into the mountains. He studies Confucian teachings under people and takes utmost care in serving his mother with filial piety. Everyone in the village knows about the filial son Zeng. His good reputation spreads throughout the town. One day, Zeng Shen went to the mountains with an axe. To chop wood and buy rice for his filial mother. Unexpectedly, a guest arrived at his home. Zeng's mother didn't know how to entertain the guest. Ashamed, she had no good plan. Having neither wine nor food nor money. Hoping her son would return quickly, but he was nowhere to be seen. Her heart was anxious, what to do? Knowing that blood is thicker than water, the mother and son are connected. Their breaths resonate with each other. She broke her finger and bit it with a ruthless heart. In Zeng Shen's heart,

the pain was unbearable. Carrying firewood, he hurried home. He knelt down and asked his mother what was the matter. Zeng's mother then began to speak. Just now, a guest came to our humble home. Because you haven't returned, there was little to entertain them. Therefore, I bit my finger to send a message for you to return. What a wise and filial Zeng! Such people are rare, and their feelings are profound. It's hard to describe in words; I hope you understand, sir.

He Yunfang, He Qinshuang, Zhu Qiu

Linji (1220) 2:15 PM to 3:00 PM

Opening Chapter: "A Small Feast in the Red Chamber" (Mimi Collection Inaugural Issue)

Daiyu's charm remains undiminished. Gradually, her spirit has recovered. She doesn't add extra adornments to her hair. Her silk clothes hang loosely on her slender waist. That Bin Yu secretly observed her first. Then, she gently used her voice to offer comfort. At this time, the autumn colors beyond the screen are beautiful. The ashes of medicine burn out, and new poems are written by the door. Look at this, the shadow on the gauze window is a natural painting. The silver candle's autumn light is a superb verse. If you deliberately stay in bed alone, I'm afraid Chang'e will laugh at your foolishness. Yingchun and her sisters smiled knowingly. Saying that one should enjoy life while it lasts. She ordered Zijuan to quickly arrange a small feast. The sisters sat in order, each taking their place without declining. The aroma of incense spread, and the golden goblets were filled. Her radiant writing flowed effortlessly. Daiyu was, however, penalized with the golden goblet. Her fair face was already flushed. Leaning on the railing, she tried to gaze at the moon in the sky. It was perfectly round and flawless at this fine time. The cold dew lightly veiled the branches of the flowers.

Zhou Zhenyu's Righteous Demon Tale

Yuanchang (1120) 12:45 AM to 1:30 AM

"Opening Chapter: Autumn Night Insect Sounds Publication" (Mimi Collection Inaugural Issue)

The autumn moon hangs over the treetops. The four walls are filled with the loneliness of autumn accompanied by insect sounds. My mother is at her spinning wheel, working tirelessly. Choosing threads and weaving is truly too exhausting. We should promote short-term labor associations. Establish preferential regulations. To prevent her from braving the cold and enduring the long, leaking nights. Calling "Brother," until her voice is hoarse. She frantically calls for her brother. Calling until her tongue is dry and her lips are parched. It's difficult, as her brother remains unseen. Causing her to carry this lifelong longing without letting go. Could it be that Brother Money's whereabouts have been distant for a long time? Could it be that news from Mexico has vanished after his departure? Therefore, her cries are loud in the middle of the night. Far away, crickets encounter much misfortune. Children pick at the cracks in the brick, searching diligently, unwilling to stop. They capture you and lock you in a tile pot, refusing to release you. Little do you know that you are being exploited for human benefit. Instead, you brandish your teeth and claws, harming your own kind. You read about battles and mutual slaughter. Showing off power and bragging about being heroes. They take advantage of others' misfortune like their kind. They are the ones who flee in defeat without a fight. Such compatriots are worthy of a deep sigh. They don't think of uniting; truly terrible. If they don't unite to resist external threats, they will regret it. I fear they won't be able to protect the beautiful land. The autumn night insect sounds are plaintive, like heavy rain echoing in the empty sky. Every sound tells of a sad and sorrowful composition. The pauses and inflections are difficult to describe. Just look at the human world and the insect world. Aren't they the same, both in a chaotic mess? Making people feel a thousand sorrows and ten thousand resentments in their hearts.

Drama 237

Haiyan Theatre Company

Jiaotong (1300) 5:45 PM to 6:30 PM

…

Xiang Yu… Zhang Rongtian

Qi Soldier Luo Ping…

Guard Hu De… Pan An

Maid… Sun Yi

Soldier A… Manfu

Soldier B… Ting

Soldier C… Yang Yiyun

Others: He Bi, Tuo Xin, Jiang Xia, Cheng Han.

Yu Ji

The tyrant we know well from history – Qin Shi Huang. At that time, he burned books and buried scholars alive. He used a brutal and dictatorial system to oppress our people. The people were oppressed to the point of having no way out, so the flames of resistance burned among them! However, their subconscious was imprisoned by the iron bricks of feudalism, preventing them from uniting the strength of the masses.

Xiang Yu, the overlord who served as a personal hero, saw this point. The lure of individual heroic status made him want to seize Qin Shi Huang's throne and replace him. So he raised a new, appealing revolutionary banner of overthrowing Qin Shi Huang, deceiving some of the laboring masses into mutually slaughtering and sacrificing themselves to win his own throne.

The laboring masses eagerly wanted to gain their own freedom and liberation! They were finally obscured and deceived by this attractive slogan, bravely overthrowing Qin Shi Huang who "burned books and buried scholars alive."

Qin Shi Huang was overthrown.

However, the revolution can also be considered a success. However, it was gradually revealed that a new, more brutal and more lewd demon was emerging!

What is unfolding here is that Xiang Yu's soldiers are realizing their own position and disregarding the sacrifice of their lives for Xiang Yu's personal quest for position and territory; they are uniting to oppose war! - To abolish war!

In the struggle for territory, Xiang Yu's own Chu state was largely occupied by Liu Bang and his forces. As midnight approached, the Han army of Liu Bang and his forces surrounded them on all sides, and from time to time some tragic songs of the Chu state drifted from their camps. The songs also aroused the homesickness of the brothers who could not return to the Chu state, and they felt as if they had lost something.

The overlord Xiang Yu was also eroded by these songs, and feeling restless, he grabbed his sword and went out madly, intending to intimidate and drive back the songs that were spreading...

This time, the soldiers were determined not to fight for Xiang Yu anymore. The guard Luo Ping was a young man with clear awareness. He and his companion Hu De, along with several other brothers, were made central figures and appeared in front of the camp to discuss the steps of launching an anti-war and peace-seeking movement of 100,000 brothers.

The beloved concubine of the overlord Xiang Yu—Yu Ji, although she used her charm to gain the favor of this demon, her physiological needs made her fall in love with the young guard Luo Ping. She was a young lady born into a noble family. Although she had a new and great style attached to her, she was still quite attached to the old, forming a dual conflicting psychology.

She protected Xiang Yu's life in order to repay Xiang Yu. But Luo Ping resolutely said: "It's either love or hate. If you stand with us, that means you don't love him, that means you hate him! Otherwise! Then you are our enemy!" This left her disappointed and "unable to argue."

On the one hand, Xiang Yu, this demon, in the instant of his impending demise, went out and acted wildly for a while before returning. He still had to drink and make merry. When the brothers raised the banner of anti-war righteousness together, it was like a final sacrifice for him... Although he still wanted to struggle!

"Sir... we are here to convey our opinions... All of us brothers are now enlightened! In the past, you tricked us into overthrowing Qin Shi Huang! Calling it "revolution!" But now that the "revolution" has succeeded, the peace we hoped for cannot be seen! And your fox tails have been revealed! The demon who slaughtered and plundered the people: the demon who oppressed the people was just overthrown, and you replaced him as an even more cruel and more lewd demon: we could have obtained peace! But you have driven us into an even more brutal and deadly war! Letting our blood build up your throne, and using our skulls to carve your crowns; you fight for power and profit, but we fly through the air in pieces, you wear brocade and eat delicacies, but we are hungry and cold! We are about to be destroyed, but you are still fighting endlessly! Sir! We are no longer willing to fill your bottomless desire pit with our limited bones! Now I tell you... the 100,000 remaining lives of us! In order to create a future society! We will no longer be your sacrifices, we will no longer fight for you!" ... They roared consciously! Making rulers like Xiang Yu tremble in front of the masses!

"This is the power of our masses!"

"…"

However, Yu Ji, struggling in a dual psychological conflict, replaced the young Luo Ping and sacrificed herself meaninglessly under the sword of the demon Xiang Yu...

Zhou Zhenyu's Righteous Demon Tale

Yuanchang (1120) Midnight 0:45 to 1:30 AM

"Opening Night's Insect Sounds" (Inaugural issue of Mimi Collection)

A solitary autumn moon upon the treetops. Four walls of autumn accompanied by lonely insects. Mother is ceaselessly at her spinning wheel. Picking threads and weaving is truly exhausting. One should advocate for shorter working hours. Stipulating preferential regulations. Lest she be chilled by the cool air, the long night all leaking away. Calling "Brother", eventually... haphazardly calling for "Brother". Calling until her tongue is dry and lips are parched. Sadly, her brother is nowhere to be seen. She clings to this lasting concern, unwilling to let go. Could it be that Brother Money's tracks have grown distant? Or perhaps all news from Mexico has vanished? Thus in the middle of the night the shouts are loud. Far off crickets encounter great misfortune. Children seek in the brick cracks, unwilling to give up. Catching and trapping you in a tile pot, not setting you free. Not realizing you are being used. Instead flexing fangs and claws harming your kind. Examining battles and mutual slaughter. Vaunting power and bravery. Seizing another's moment of weakness, like their type. They are routed and flee. Such compatriots are lamentable. Failing to unite, truly a disaster. Unless they unite and resist outside threats, it is feared they cannot keep this great land. Autumn night's insect sounds are keen, like torrential rain echoing in the empty sky. Each sound conveys sorrowful melodies, nuanced and soaring, difficult to describe. Just look at the human world and the insect world. Are they not the same, an utter mess. Making people feel a thousand sorrows and ten thousand regrets.

Drama 239

Haiyan Theatre Company

Jiaotong (1300) 5:45 PM to 6:30 PM

…

Xiang Yu… Zhang Rongtian

Qi Soldier Luo Ping…

Guard Hu De… Pan An

Maid… Sun Yi

Soldier A… Manfu

Soldier B… Ting

Soldier C… Yang Yiyun

Others: He Bi, Tuo Xin, Jiang Xia, Cheng Han.

Yu Ji

The tyrant well known throughout history - Qin Shi Huang. At that time, he burned books and buried scholars. Employing a brutal authoritarian system, oppressing our people. The people, oppressed until there was no path left. Thus amongst them, anger burned. However, their subconscious was constrained by feudal iron walls, preventing them from unifying the people's strength.

As the personal heroic overlord - Xiang Yu, saw this. The selfish desire for heroic glory made him want to usurp the throne from Qin Shi Huang. Thus he raised a new seductive banner to overthrow Qin Shi Huang, deceiving some of the common people, for them to slaughter each other, to be sacrificed, for him to fight for his own throne.

The common people wished urgently to gain their own freedom and liberation! Finally, they were deceived and misled by this sweet sounding slogan, bravely overthrowing Qin Shi Huang who “burned books and buried scholars”.

Qin Shi Huang was overthrown.

However, the revolution was also considered a success. However, it was gradually becoming apparent that a new demon, even more cruel and lewd, was appearing!

What is being revealed here is that Xiang Yu's soldiers were realizing their own position and ignoring sacrificing themselves for Xiang Yu's personal battle for position and territory. Unifying themselves to oppose war! – To abolish war!

To fight for territory, Xiang Yu’s homeland of Chu had already been occupied in a large part by Liu Bang and his forces. As midnight approaches, the Han army of Liu Bang and his forces are surrounding them on all sides, and at times from their camps, there floated tragic songs of the Chu homeland, that aroused the emotions of the brothers who cannot return to Chu. Feeling as if they had lost something.

The overlord Xiang Yu also became corroded by these songs, becoming restless he took his sword and went out madly, attempting to scare away those diffusing songs…

This time, the soldier brothers had resolved to no longer fight for Xiang Yu. The guard Luo Ping was a young man with clear understanding, he and his companion Hu De and a few other brothers were made the central figures, appearing before the curtain to discuss the steps to launch a mass anti-war movement seeking peace for the hundred thousand brothers.

The beloved concubine of the overlord Xiang Yu - Yu Ji, although she used her seductive charms to obtain the joy of this demon, her physiological desires made her fall in love with the young guard Luo Ping. She was a young lady born into a noble family, although she had a new and great style attached to her, she was still quite attached to the old, forming a dual conflicting psychology.

She protected Xiang Yu’s life, as repayment to Xiang Yu. But Luo Ping firmly said: “It is either love or hate. If you stand with us, that means you don’t love him, that means you hate him! Otherwise! Then you are our enemy!” Which left her disappointed and “unable to argue.”

On one hand, Xiang Yu this demon, at the instant of his impending fall, went out to boast and show off for a time before returning. Still needing to drink and make merry… When the brothers all together raised the righteous flag of anti-war, it was as if they were making a final sacrifice. … Although he still wanted to struggle!

“Sir… we have come to convey our opinions… All of us brothers now are awakened! Before, you deceived us into overthrowing Qin Shi Huang! Calling it “revolution!” But: now that “revolution” has succeeded, the peace that we wished for cannot be seen! And your fox tail has been revealed! Slaughtering the people, plundering the people: the demon who oppressed the people had only just been overthrown, and you have replaced him to become an even more cruel and more lewd demon: We could have obtained peace! But instead, you have driven us into an even more brutal, towards destruction in war! Allowing our blood to build your throne, using our skulls to carve your crowns; you fight for power and gain, while we are torn to pieces, you wear fine clothes and have delicious food, while we are cold and starving! We are on the verge of destruction, but you are still engaged in endless battles! Sir! We are no longer willing to fill your bottomless pit of desire with our limited bones! I tell you now… the remaining 100,000 lives of us! In order to create a future society! We will no longer be your sacrifices, we will no longer fight for you!” … Also consciously roaring! Causing rulers of Xiang Yu’s kind to tremble before the masses!
